    -   2.1[08/13/2020 - Using your TigerStop with STRATUS!](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746/Package+Cut+Lists#PackageCutLists-08%2F13%2F2020-UsingyourTigerStopwithSTRATUS!)

## Generate Cut Lists

On the Package's Cut List tab, use the **Generate Cut Lists** button to send a nested cut list to the STRATUS Workstation application that controls the TigerStop tool.

1.  Before you can generate a cut list targeted to the TigerStop, you must first configure a **[Tool](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220225/Tools+Admin)**, **[Division](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/103317524/Processor+Admin)**, and **[Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408/Station+Admin)** for the TigerStop. 
2.  In order to enable the **Generate Cut List** button on the package's Cut Lists tab, the package must be in a tracking status where **Can Cut List** option is checked. Click the Tracking tab to change the tracking status. See the **[Tracking Statuses](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761)** article for more information. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-15-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630696552116&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=175)
3.  With a valid tracking status set for the package, the package's **Generate Cut List** button on the **Cut List** **tab** is enabled.
4.  Click the **Generate Cut List** button. Before the cut list displays STRATUS makes several checks.
    1.  **Check 1** - The cut list is checked to determine if all parts in the package are in a “Can Cut List” tracking status.
        1.  **Yes** - If all parts are in a “Can Cut List” tracking status, go to Check 2.
            
        2.  **No** \- If not, a dialog similar to the following will display indicating how many parts are not in a “Can Cut List” tracking status.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2022-5-25_14-48-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653508128231&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
            1.  **Cancel** \- Click **Cancel** to stop the process and change the tracking status of parts that are not in a “Can Cut List” tracking status.
                
            2.  **Generate** \- Click **Generate** to continue with Check 2.
                
    2.  **Check 2** - The cut list is checked to determine if any of the parts have already been cut.
        
        **There are several ways to determine if a part has been cut:**
        
        1.  The cut part’s tracking status is updated to **Cut**. In the STRATUS Workstation, the **Apply Tracking Status on Done** can automatically apply a tracking status. If this tracking status is **Cut**, then the part will be considered cut. **Note:** Be sure to verify that your **Apply Tracking Status on Done** tracking status is Cut and does not have the **Can Cut List** checkbox checked.  
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-5-25_14-49-40.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653508181292&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=651&height=250)
            
        2.  If any part is not in a **Can Cut List** tracking status, it will be considered cut.
            
        3.  If STRATUS.Part.CutDT property is populated, the part will be considered cut.
            
        4.  If STRATUS.Part.IsCut property is 1, the part will be considered cut.
            
        5.  If the Tracking comment for a part includes the word cut, the part will be considered cut. 
            
            **Did STRATUS detect that a part has already been cut?**
            
        6.  **No** \- If no parts have been cut, the cut list will be generated.
            
        7.  **Yes** \- If a part has already been cut, a message similar to the following will display.  
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2022-5-25_14-59-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1653508773595&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
            1.  **Cancel** \- Click **Cancel** to cancel the process of generating the cut list.
            2.  **Include cut item** \- Click the **Include cut items** button to include parts that have already been cut. This is used to recut parts.
            3.  **Exclude** \- Click the **Exclude cut items** button to exclude parts that have already been
                
5.  The cut lists will display.
    1.  If a cutlist has been sent to a station and there have not been any changes, a new cut list will not be regenerated.
        
6.  Once the cut list displays the Cut Lists table will be populated.  
    
    1.  Group by Area
        1.  **Unchecked** (Default) - When unchecked, and the **Generate Cut Lists** button is clicked:![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-9-9_10-30-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662737419562&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=569)
            1.  **Blank** - Area will remain blank if there are parts in the cutlist that are not associated with any area.
                
            2.  **Multiple Areas** - **Multiple Areas** will be displayed if there are multiple areas in that cutlist. On hover over **Multiple Areas**, each area in the cutlist will be displayed.
                
            3.  **One Area** - The area will be displayed if there is only one area associated to that size and material.
                
        2.  **Checked** \- When checked and the **Generate Cut Lists** button is clicked, a new list will be generated for parts having the same material and size, but different areas.  
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-9-9_10-31-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1662737475352&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=624)
            1.  **Each Area** - A record for each area will be displayed if there are multiple areas for a specific size and material (Ex. Material = Carbon Steel, Size = 3/8).
                
            2.  **Undefined** - **Undefined** will be displayed if there are parts for a specific size and material that are not associated to any area.
                
        3.  **Notes:**
            1.  The resulting cut lists inside of STRATUS Workstation will not utilize the Area but the cut lists can be sent separately as needed.  
                
            2.  **Error**: The given key was not present in the dictionary. When this message is displayed, it means that the **Group by Area** checkbox is checked, at least one part in the cut list has been assigned to an area, but other parts have not. Go back to the Package's Viewer and add all parts to the area under Actions > Areas.   
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-29-59.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634049000276&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=400&height=125) 
    2.  The Cut Lists interface:  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-28-43.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630697325049&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=300)
        1.  **Default Sort Order** - The default sort order is by material, size, and then area if selected.
        2.  **Generate Cut Lists** - The **Generate Cut Lists button remains enabled**. You can overwrite the existing cut list by clicking the Generate Cut List button again.
        3.  **Select** - Click the **Select checkbox** to select all Cut Lists. With multiple Cut Lists checked, the Station can be changed for all checked Cut Lists and the **Update multiple records** dialog will display and including the number of records to be updated. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2023-9-22_9-1-6.png?version=1&modificationDate=1695391267725&cacheVersion=1&api=v2) 
        4.  **Material** - Displays the material as specified in either the parts:
            1.  Properties.  
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-1-59.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634047321181&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=450&height=349)
            2.  Overridden Property in the part's **Cut List Mappings** under Admin > Company > Part Template > Cut List Mappings.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-1-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634047266782&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=900&height=314)
        5.  **Size** \-  The default Size for pipe parts is the diameter formatted as fractional inches or mm in metric. Displays the size as specified in either the parts:
            1.  Properties.  
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-3-54.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634047435578&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=450&height=283)
            2.  Overridden Property in the part's **Cut List Mappings** under Admin > Company > Part Template > Cut List Mappings.  
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-4-58.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634047500749&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=900&height=314)
        6.  **Area** - The STRATUS.Part.BIMArea value.  
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-10-12_9-7-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1634047672289&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=426&height=250)
        7.  **\# Items** - Number of like items included in the cut list.
        8.  **Total Length** - The Total Length for all like items in the cut list.
        9.  **Station** - A default **Station** will be selected. If a Material has been configured and associated with a Station, STRATUS will detect the material and select the Station. Otherwise, change the station as needed. The tool (read only) is associated with the Station will display. See the [**Materials (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215351308/Materials+Admin) article for more information.
        10.  **Tool** - The selected Station should be associated with a Tool. If not, the Tool will be blank. A Tool is associated with a Station under Admin > Company > Stations. See the **[Station (Admin)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408/Station+Admin)** article for more information.
        11.  **Status** - The **Status** of each cut list. See the [**Send Cut List to Station (STRATUS Workstation)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746/Package+Cut+Lists#PackageCutLists-SendCutListtoStation(STRATUSWorkstation)) section on how the Status changes. 
        12.  **Modified By** - **Modified By** is updated once the cut list has been cut using the tool and the Status is Complete.
        13.  **Modified**  - **Modified** is updated once the cut list has been cut using the tool and the Status is Complete. 
        14.  **Delete** a Cut List ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-9-55.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542053397937&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=29&height=27)\- The **Delete** button will remove the item from the Cut Lists tab. If the **Send Cut List to Station** button had already been clicked, the Delete button will also remove the item from the queue of the STRATUS Workstation application and from the Shops > Station > Tool > Queued Items list. The progress of the cut list is not retained so parts already cut will could be cut a second time if the item is resent to a cutting station. 
        15.  **Unassign from Station** ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-7-42.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542053265227&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)\- After the **Send Cut List to Station** button has been clicked (row 1 above), the Cut List file will be sent to the queue in the STRATUS Workstation application and the Cut List will also display in the Shops > Station > Tool > Queued Items list. To remove the cut list from this station, click the **Unassign from Station** button from either Package's Cut Lists tab or from the Shops \> Station > Tool > Queued Items list. The progress of the cut list is retained so parts already cut will not be cut a second time when resent to a cutting station. In addition, the cut list will be retained on the Cut Lists tab ready to be sent to a station. 
        16.  The **Print Labels** ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-13-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542053589657&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)\- The **Print Labels** button can be used along with **[STRATUS Print](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974545/Label+Printing+for+Zebra+ZPL+compatible+printers)** and a ZPL compatible printer.  The labels for any cut list item can be printed to a selected ZPL printer regardless of how the cut list was generated.
            1.  Note: If you are sending the cut list to the STRATUS Workstation application, you have the option of printing the labels after each part is cut. If this is the case, you do not need to print labels using this button.

## Send Cut List to Station (STRATUS Workstation) 

1.  The checkbox of at least one cut list item needs to be checked in order for the **Send Cut List to Station** button to become enabled.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-38-54.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630697936721&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=380)
2.  Verify that the correct Station has been selected and then click the **Send Cut List to Station** button. If you configured a Material and associated it with a Station, STRATUS will detect the material and automatically select the Station.
    1.  The cut list will be sent to the queue and the **Send Cut List to Station** button will be disabled until another cut list is checked.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-42-12.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630698133812&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=386)
    2.  The page will refresh.
    3.  The checkbox for any previously checked cut list item will be disabled.
    4.  The **Status** will change to In Progress \[0%\] and the **Unassign from Station** **button** will be enabled.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-43-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630698234217&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=382)
    5.  The Cut List item is now in the TigerStop queue in the STRATUS Workstation application.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2021-9-3_14-45-21.png?version=1&modificationDate=1630698323236&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=584)
3.  **Note:**  If a user changes the name of a package after sending a cut list to the STRATUS Workstation, the old package name will continue to display in the STRATUS Workstation. To resolve this issue, delete the cut list and resend it to the STRATUS Workstation.

## Generate .PCF PypeServer Cut List File

### Automated

Please review the **[AutoCAD Publish and Import](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/208568421/AutoCAD+Publish+and+Import)** article that notes the requirement to have installed **Fabrication CADmep version 2019.1** in order to generate a.PCF file.

A .PCF file can be automatically generated when a package Tracking Status changes. The automation is linked to the Package Category.

To automatically generate a MAJ / PCF file when a Package Tracking Status changes:

1.  Under Admin > Company > Package Categories, the Generate MAJ and PCF on Tracking Status options display for each package category.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-10-13.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427014448&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=385)
    
2.  By default, the Generate MAJ or PCF is set to Off. For each Package Category, one tracking status can be selected to generate a MAJ and/or a PCF file. **Note**: These files can still be generated on the Packages Dashboard in the Output column.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-10-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427053798&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=800&height=338)
    
    1.  **Off** - Neither MAJ or PCF files will be automatically created for the Package Category.
        
    2.  **Any tracking status** - When the package tracking status is changed to the selected tracking status, the process to generate a MAJ and/or PCF will begin and the file will display in the Package’s > Attachments when it has completed. There is no visual indication that this process has started.
        
3.  In this example, for the Fabrication Release Package Category, the **Issued for Fabrication** tracking status is selected for both the **Generate MAJ on Tracking Status** and the **Generate PCF on Tracking Status**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-11-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427108959&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
4.  After changing a package tracking status to **Issued For Fabrication**, the process to generate a MAJ and/or PCF will begin and the file(s) will display in the Package’s > Attachments when the process has completed. There is no visual indication that this process has started.
    
5.  The MAJ and/or PCF will display in the Package’s > Attachments.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-13-48.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427229610&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=355)
    
6.  After clicking the file to download, a separate page will display. Click the **Download** button to save the file to your computer. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-23-51.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427832632&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=600&height=295)
7.  Your normal .PCF workflow can continue.

### Manual

Please review the **[AutoCAD Publish and Import](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/208568421/AutoCAD+Publish+and+Import)** article that notes the requirement to have installed **Fabrication CADmep version 2019.1** in order to generate a.PCF file.

To generate a package's .PCF file:

1.  Go to the Packages Dashboard and locate the package.
2.  Click the PCF button ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-32-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542054775149&cacheVersion=1&api=v2) under Output associated with the package. The file will generate.   
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-4-48.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542060290745&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=906&height=250)
3.  Once the PCF file is generated:
    1.  It can be downloaded from the attachment icon on the Packages Dashboard.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-38-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542055101571&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=300&height=304)
    2.  Or, it can be downloaded from the package's Attachments tab.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_14-39-39.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542055182228&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=638&height=296)
4.  After clicking the file to download, a separate page will display. Click the **Download** button to save the file to your computer.   
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-10-29.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542060632542&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
5.  Your normal .PCF workflow can continue.

## Generate .MAJ CamDuct Cut List File

### Automated

Please review the **[AutoCAD Publish and Import](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/208568421/AutoCAD+Publish+and+Import)** article that notes the requirement to have installed **Fabrication CADmep version 2019.1** in order to generate a.MAJ file.

An .MAJ file can be automatically generated when a package Tracking Status changes. The automation is linked to the Package Category.

To automatically generate a MAJ / PCF file when a Package Tracking Status changes:

1.  Under Admin > Company > Package Categories, the Generate MAJ and PCF on Tracking Status options display for each package category.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-10-13.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427014448&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=385)
    
2.  By default, the Generate MAJ or PCF is set to Off. For each Package Category, one tracking status can be selected to generate a MAJ and/or a PCF file. **Note**: These files can still be generated on the Packages Dashboard in the Output column.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-10-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427053798&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=800&height=338)
    
    1.  **Off** - Neither MAJ or PCF files will be automatically created for the Package Category.
        
    2.  **Any tracking status** - When the package tracking status is changed to the selected tracking status, the process to generate a MAJ and/or PCF will begin and the file will display in the Package’s > Attachments when it has completed. There is no visual indication that this process has started.
        
3.  In this example, for the Fabrication Release Package Category, the **Issued for Fabrication** tracking status is selected for both the **Generate MAJ on Tracking Status** and the **Generate PCF on Tracking Status**.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-11-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427108959&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
4.  After changing a package tracking status to **Issued For Fabrication**, the process to generate a MAJ and/or PCF will begin and the file(s) will display in the Package’s > Attachments when the process has completed. There is no visual indication that this process has started.
    
5.  The MAJ and/or PCF will display in the Package’s > Attachments.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-13-48.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649427229610&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=355)
    
6.  After clicking the file to download, a separate page will display. Click the **Download** button to save the file to your computer. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2022-4-8_9-29-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1649428198171&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
7.  From here you can use your normal workflow for processing these file types. See the **[Post MAJ Download Workflow](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746/Package+Cut+Lists#PackageCutLists-PostMAJDownloadWorkflow)** section for more information.

### Manual

Please review the **[AutoCAD Publish and Import](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/208568421/AutoCAD+Publish+and+Import)** article that notes the requirement to have installed **Fabrication CADmep version 2019.1** in order to generate a.MAJ file.

To generate a package's .MAJ file:

1.  Go to the Packages Dashboard and locate the package.
2.  Click the MAJ button ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-0-56.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542060059143&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=28&height=28) under Output associated with the package. The file will generate.   
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-19-27.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542061169684&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=900&height=295)
3.  Once the MAJ file is generated:
    1.  It can be downloaded from the attachment icon on the Packages Dashboard.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-8-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542060539783&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=262&height=250)
    2.  Or, it can be downloaded from the package's Attachments tab.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-17-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542061023671&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=746&height=250)
4.  After clicking the file to download, a separate page will display. Click the **Download** button to save the file to your computer.   
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-21-22.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542061286307&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
5.  From here you can use your normal workflow for processing these file types. See the **[Post MAJ Download Workflow](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746/Package+Cut+Lists#PackageCutLists-PostMAJDownloadWorkflow)** section for more information.

## Post MAJ Download Workflow

1.  Open the downloaded MAJ file in CADmep using the OPENJOB command and the Fab Viewer will display where you can:
    1.  View the part status from STRATUS.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-26-28.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542061591553&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=576&height=393)
    2.  And, if under Admin > Company > Setting > Specific to AutoCAD > the **Property To Map To Package Name** is configured, and the **Property To Map To QR Code** is configured, they will be populated under the Custom Data tab.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-12_16-27-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542061627657&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=240&height=344)
2.  In the Fab Viewer, click OK and then click the **Top** view to display the MAJ file. Then you can also view the properties and custom properties of the part.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-11-15_8-58-9.png?version=1&modificationDate=1542293892033&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=528&height=454)
3.  **QR Code Link:** Under Item Properties > Links, the links the STRATUS QR Codes for Part QR Code, Assembly QR Code, and Package QR Code are always in this order if the QR Code type exists:
    1.  Links #1 = Part QR Code
        
    2.  Links #2 = Assembly QR Code
        
    3.  Links #3 = Package QR Code
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/plugins/servlet/confluence/placeholder/error?i18nKey=editor.placeholder.broken.image&locale=en_GB&version=2 "Missing required attribute: {http://atlassian.com/resource/identifier}value")
        
    4.  When clicked the QR Code Scanned page will display.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/plugins/servlet/confluence/placeholder/error?i18nKey=editor.placeholder.broken.image&locale=en_GB&version=2 "Missing required attribute: {http://atlassian.com/resource/identifier}value")
        

## Generate T-Drill Cut List

## Import Cut List - Upload the file that contains the cut lists

To import a cut list from a .CSV or .TXT cut list file your STRATUS administrator must first configure an **[Import Mapping](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170196993/Import+Mappings+Admin)** under **Admin > Company > Import Mappings.** This configuration defines your import file header row and maps the data fields. The actual cut list file you select below must conform to the Import Mapping settings. **Note**: The .CSV or .TXT file must include a column whose header is Size and another column whose header is Length.

1.  From a Package Detail, click the **Cut Lists** tab.
2.  Click the **Import Cut Lists** button. 
3.  Select the **Upload the file that contains the cut lists** option.
4.  Click the **Browse** button and locate the cut list file to be uploaded.   
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-8-14_14-4-34.png?version=1&modificationDate=1534273476794&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=270&height=396) 
5.  This file must conform to the Import Mapping setting under **Admin > Company > Import Mappings.** STRATUS will recognize whether it is a CSV or TXT file type and select the correct Import Mapping.
6.  Once the cut list file has been uploaded, click the **Import** button and the cut list will display. In this case, 2 cut lists for 2 different sizes were imported.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-8-14_14-6-46.png?version=1&modificationDate=1534273608449&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=432&height=98)
7.  You can either:
    1.  Click the **Print Labels** button to print to a ZPL printer, or,
    2.  If you have a TigerStop, select a Station, check one or more cut list rows, and then click the **Send Cut List to Station**. 

## Import Cut List - Select the report that contains the cut lists

To import a cut list from a .CSV or .TXT cut list file your STRATUS administrator must first configure an Import Mapping under **Admin > Company > Import Mappings.** This configuration defines your import file header row and maps the data fields. The actual cut list file you select below must conform to the Import Mapping settings. **Note**: The .CSV or .TXT file must include a column whose header is Size and another column whose header is Length.

1.  From a Package Detail, click the **Cut Lists** tab.
2.  Click the **Import Cut Lists** button. 
3.  Select the **Select the report that contains the cut lists** option. Select a report in the drop-down list. If you have more than one import mapping, select the import mapping that was configured to be used with the report.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-8-14_16-31-55.png?version=1&modificationDate=1534282317160&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=300&height=442)
4.  Click **Import**. The Cut List will display.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166723746/image2018-8-14_16-51-31.png?version=1&modificationDate=1534283493120&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=908&height=250)
5.  You can either:
    1.  Click the **Print Labels** button to print to a ZPL printer, or,
    2.  If you have a TigerStop, select a Station, check one or more cut list rows, and then click the **Send Cut List to Station**.

# Package Items - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Package Items tab displays consolidated table views into the package’s assemblies and parts. By default, the package’s Assemblies display in the top table and the Parts display in the bottom table. In addition, each assembly can be expanded to display its parts. Each table displays information based on the default report or a custom report. The parts table can be further filtered by parts in an Assembly or Loose parts.

---
The Package Items tab displays consolidated table views into the package’s assemblies and parts. By default, the package’s Assemblies display in the top table and the Parts display in the bottom table. In addition, each assembly can be expanded to display its parts. Each table displays information based on the default report or a custom report. The parts table can be further filtered by parts in an Assembly or Loose parts.

-   1[Project Role Permissions](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-ProjectRolePermissions)
-   2[Filters](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-Filters)
-   3[Assemblies Table](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-AssembliesTable)
-   4[Parts Table](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-PartsTable)
    -   4.1[Lightning Catalog Parts](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-LightningCatalogParts)
-   5[Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-Videos)

By default, the Packages > Item tab displays the Assemblies section and Parts section using a Default report for both the Assembly Report, Part Report, and the Report (Parts section).![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-6-24_16-27-20.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656106041622&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1230&height=250)

## Project Role Permissions

Packages > Items permission are controlled under Admin > Company Project Roles > Modify Packages.   
![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-6-24_16-43-49.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656107030220&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=400&height=434) 

-   **Attachments** \- When checked the project role can add an attachment to an assembly.
-   **Modify Packages** - When checked the project role can add/remove assemblies to/from a package.
    
-   **Remove** - When checked the project role can view the Remove assemblies and parts from the package.
    
-   **View** \- When checked the project role can view the Assemblies > Dashboard, including Attachments.
    

## Filters

1.  **Filters**
    
    1.  **Project** - The project name.
        
    2.  **Model** - The model name.
        
    3.  **Packages** - The package name and number. All packages that include the assembly are displayed including a link to the package and the ability to add/remove the assembly to/from packages. 
        
        1.  **Add** \- To add the assembly to a package, click the drop-down and select the package. Packages that an assembly cannot be added to due to rules (Ex. Package must be in a "Can Package" tracking status or the assembly can only be added to a Package in a Package Category once) are disabled.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-6-24_16-32-36.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656106357812&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=488&height=250)
        2.  **Remove** \- To remove the assembly from a package, click the x associated with the package.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2022-6-24_16-39-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656106791461&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        3.  After the Packages dialog save button is clicked, a message similar to the following will display letting you know the name of the assembly(s) and the name of the package(s) impacted by the modification.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2022-6-15_15-52-6.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656106847308&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2022-6-15_15-53-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656106847401&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
    4.  **Tracking Status Division and Group** - If a Division has been selected for the package, the Division (Ex. Duct Shop) and Tracking Status Group \[Shop\] will display to the left of the Tracking Status. 
        
    5.  **Tracking Status** - The current package tracking status.
        
    6.  **Category** - The Package Category.
        
    7.  **Show** \- Show controls the data tables (All, Assemblies, or Parts) that will display on the page.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2022-4-18_8-18-11.png?version=1&modificationDate=1650287893151&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        
        1.  **All**
            
            1.  **Assemblies data table** - Displays a data table for the package’s Assemblies. **Note:** Any assembly can be expanded to display its parts.
                
            2.  **Parts data table** - Displays a separate data table (below) for the package’s Parts.
                
            3.  **Reports** - Displays the **Assembly Report** and **Part Report** option lists.
                
        2.  **Assemblies**
            
            1.  **Assemblies data table** - Displays a data table for the package’s Assemblies. The package’s Parts table does not display. **Note:** Any assembly can be expanded to display its parts.
                
            2.  **Reports** - Displays the **Assembly Report** and **Part Report** option lists.
                
        3.  **Parts**
            
            1.  **Parts data table** - Displays the data table for the package’s Parts. The package’s Assemblies table does not display.
                
            2.  **Part Report drop-down lists** \- In the Report selection row, the Assembly Report and Part Report option lists both display if All is selected under Show.
                
            3.  **Show**\- When Parts is selected under Show, the Show drop-down list displays and provides users with options for how the parts display:
                
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2022-4-18_8-30-34.png?version=1&modificationDate=1650288636184&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
                
                1.  **All** - All parts in an assembly and loose parts will display.
                    
                2.  **In Assembly** - Only parts that are included in an assembly will display.
                    
                3.  **Loose** - Only loose parts (not included in an assembly) will display.
                    
            4.  **Report** \- Displays the **Part Report** option list.
                
    8.  **Search** \- Search text fields in the Items list.
        

## Assemblies Table

1.  **Assemblies table** (If Shown)
    
    1.  **Assembly Report** - The selected report is used to display the package’s assemblies.
        
        1.  **Default** - By default, the **Default Assembly Report** will display. This report is not editable and includes the following columns.
            
            1.  **Show (Multiple Entry Selection and Action)** - Multiple entries (rows) can be selected and then an action can be taken on those entries (Ex. Update Tracking Status, edit an editable field, and Delete). See the **[Multiple Entry Selection and Action FAQ](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action)** for more information and examples.
            2.  **Expand/Collapse** - The first column includes an expand/collapse button. When expanded the assembly parts will display within the selected Part Report.  
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-4-18_9-12-6.png?version=1&modificationDate=1650291128318&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1050&height=348)
                
            3.  **Assembly Name** - The Name of the Assembly and a link to the Assembly in the Assemblies > Viewer tab. The list of assemblies are ordered alphabetically.
                
            4.  **Parts** \- The total number of parts in the assembly.
                
            5.  **Hours** \- The total number of actual hours applied to the assembly.
                
            6.  **Status** \- The current Status of the assembly. Edit that status by clicking the status name link. The current Tracking Status for the Package displays in the package filter row. Individual package assemblies will initially have the same tracking status as the package but can be changed independently to track work on the package in the items grid. A package can only be edited when it is in a "Can Package" tracking status. "Can Package" is a setting associated with the tracking status that tells STRATUS whether or not the package can be edited or not.
                
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-4-18_8-22-43.png?version=1&modificationDate=1650288165200&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=350&height=296)
                
                1.  **Note**: The ability to select multiple assemblies and change their status simultaneously has been removed. Let us know if that feature was useful.
                    
            7.  **Tasks** - If a Task Definition has been defined, the tasks associated with the assembly will display. Each task can be clicked to change from red (To Do) to green (Done).
                
            8.  **Attachments** - Attach a file to the assembly record.
                
                1.  **Note:** Attachment to a part can be viewed when the part is selected under Model > Viewer > Actions > Attachments.
                    
            9.  **Remove** - To delete an assembly from the package, click the **Remove** button. The selected assembly will be removed from the package and will be available to add to another package within the same package category.
                
                1.  **Note**: Only loose parts can be removed from a Package, therefore, there is no option to remove a part from an Assembly in the Package’s > Items tab. See the Assembly > Viewer article for removing a part from an assembly.
                    
        2.  **Custom Reports** - Additional custom reports display in the Report drop-down list where under Admin > Company > Reports the report:
            
            1.  Item Type = Assembly
                
            2.  Package Viewer = checked
                
        3.  **Filter / Sort the data table**
            
            1.  **Filter** - Click the Filter icon in the column header to Filter the list.
                
            2.  **Sort** - Click the arrows in the column header to sort the list by the column.
                

## Parts Table

The Parts data table displays a list of parts included in the package. If the model associated with the package has been published along with its Fabrication database, the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** button will be enabled which can be used to add items from the Fabrication database catalog to the package and automatically published.

1.  **Parts table** (If Shown)
    
    1.  ****Add Lightning Catalog Parts**** - The ********Add Lightning Catalog Parts******** button will be enabled if the model associated with the package has been published along with its Fabrication database. This this enabled, users can add items from the Fabrication database catalog to the package and automatically published. See the **[Lightning Catalog Parts](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166658049/Package+Items#PackageItems-LightningCatalogParts)** section for more information.
    2.  **Show (Multiple Entry Selection and Action)** - Multiple entries (rows) can be selected and then an action can be taken on those entries (Ex. Update Tracking Status, edit an editable field, and Delete). See the **[Multiple Entry Selection and Action FAQ](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1963720705/Multiple+Entry+Selection+and+Action)** for more information and examples.
    3.  **Default** - By default, the **Default Parts Report** will display. This report is not editable and includes the following columns.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-42-51.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224173319&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        
        1.  **Description** \- The Description field is extracted from the part’s AutoCAD/Revit database.
            
        2.  **Assembly Name** - The name of the assembly to which the part belongs. Loose parts will not have an assembly name.
            
        3.  **Hours** \-
            
        4.  **Status** \- The current Status of the Part. Edit that status by clicking the status name link. The current Tracking Status for the Package displays in the package filter row. Individual package parts will initially have the same tracking status as the package but can be changed independently to track work on the package in the items grid. A package can only be edited when it is in a "Can Package" tracking status. "Can Package" is a setting associated with the tracking status that tells STRATUS whether or not the package can be edited or not.
            
            1.  **Note**: The ability to select multiple assemblies and change their status simultaneously has been removed. Let us know if that feature was useful.
                
        5.  **Remove** \- To delete a package part, click the **Remove** button. The selected part will be removed from the package and will be available to add to another package within the same package category. **Note**: In the Items tab, a part cannot be removed from an assembly that is included in a package.
            
    4.  **Show** - See the Filters section above.
        
    5.  **Custom Reports** - Additional custom reports display in the Report drop-down list where under Admin > Company > Reports the report:
        
        1.  Item Type = Part
            
        2.  Package Viewer = checked
            
            1.  **Quantity column** - The Quantity column will display automatically in a custom report when it is configured with **Merge Like Values** and **Show Quantity** set to  “Yes”.  
                ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/166658049/image2022-7-1_15-48-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1656708481898&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=458&height=250)
    6.  **Filter / Sort the data table**
        
        1.  **Filter** - Click the Filter icon in the column header to Filter the list.
            
        2.  **Sort** - Click the arrows in the column header to sort the list by the column.
            

### Lightning Catalog Parts

The **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** button and dialog has been added to the Packages > Viewer > Parts data table. This feature is enabled when a model has been published along with its Fabrication database. Items from the Fabrication database catalog can be added to the package and automatically published.

**GTP Lightning application:**

-   Can be downloaded from the [**STRATUS Help**](https://www.gtpstratus.com/home/help) page.
    
-   Can be used with both STRATUS and Field Orderz to publish and synchronize Autodesk Fabrication databases to the GTP Cloud.
    
-   Enables Fabrication Services to be used by Field Orderz for sketching and fitting input.
    
-   Improves the speed of the STRATUS model publish process.
    
-   Enables STRATUS publishing for users without access to the Fabrication database.
    
-   Is used to add Fabrication Catalog parts to a package (see below).
    

To use the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** feature:

1.  Before the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** feature is enabled, the model’s Fabrication database must be published using the **GTP Lightning** app.
    
    1.  Download **GTP Lightning** from the [**STRATUS Help**](https://www.gtpstratus.com/home/help) page.
        
    2.  For more information about how to configure download and install GTP Lightning see the following article:
        
2.  Open a package whose model has been published using **GTP Lightning**. Under Packages > Viewer > Items > Parts, the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** button will display.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-47-44.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224466334&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
3.  Click the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** button. The Lightning Catalog displays an **Add Part(s) to PackageName** dialog similar to the following.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-48-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224495947&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    
    1.  **1\. Filter**
        
        1.  **Search** - Search for text included in a part in the Fabrication database.
            
        2.  **Bought Out**
            
            1.  **Unchecked (Default)** - When unchecked, **Bought Out** items will not display.
                
            2.  **Checked** - When checked, **Bought Out** items will display.
                
        3.  **Profile** - The Profile drop-down displays all of the authoring tool profiles available when the Fabrication database was published. The **Default** profile will display by default. The selected Profile will be used to filter the parts in the catalog.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-48-38.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224520519&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
        4.  **Service Type** - The Service Type drop-down includes service types.
            
        5.  **Service** \- The Service drop-down includes parent service groups (bold) and child services.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-49-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224545053&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
        6.  **Material** \- Displays the list of materials.
            
        7.  **Manufacturer** \- Displays the list of manufacturers.
            
        8.  **Connector** \- Displays the list of connectors.
            
        9.  **Part Type** - The Part Type drop-down filter only includes the following options:
            
            1.  **Any** - Displays any part.
                
            2.  **Fittings** \- Only displays parts that are fittings.
                
            3.  **Straights** \- Only displays parts that are straights.
                
        10.  **Quick Add** - Displays the top 10 added parts determined by the number of times the exact part was added to a package.
            
    2.  **2\. Select (###)**
        
        1.  The **Select (###)** will display the number of parts in the filter.
            
        2.  Expand the catalog to locate and select parts. Once selected the part will display in the **Configure and Add** section and an image of the part will display if one is in the Fabrication database.
            
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-49-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224575287&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            
    3.  **3\. Configure and Add** - For a selected item:
        
        1.  **QTY** - For the item to be added, set the quantity.
            
        2.  **Size** \- For the item to be added, if the Fabrication database includes multiple sizes, each one can be separately selected. A new size can be selected and the **Add plus button** clicked to add multiple sizes.
            
        3.  **Add plus button** - Click the **Add** button to add the part to the data table.
            
        4.  **Remove** \- In the Remove column, click the **remove** button (red) to remove an item from the data table.
            
        5.  **Publish Items to STRATUS**
            
            1.  After one part is added, the **Publish Items to STRATUS** button will be enabled.
                
            2.  Click the **Publish Items to STRATUS** button to publish the selected catalog items to the STRATUS package. The publish process will extract the needed properties for STRATUS from the Fabrication database.
                
            3.  During the publish process, the package will be locked.
                
    4.  Once the **Add Lightning Catalog Parts** publish process is complete:
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-4-11_9-49-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1681224599377&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        
        1.  The package will be unlocked.
            
        2.  The parts will display in the Packages > Viewer > Parts data table.
            
        3.  The publish parts tracking Status’s will be assigned the first **Applies to Part** Tracking Status (Ex. Design).
            
4.  To remove a catalog part from the package:
    1.  Click the Remove button. Multiple parts can be removed by checking the row checkbox and then clicking the **Remove** button for one of them.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-10-4_13-27-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1696444079154&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  A prompt similar to the following will displays.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/166658049/image2023-10-4_13-28-34.png?version=1&modificationDate=1696444116363&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    3.  Click **Remove** and the parts will be removed from the package.

## Videos

# Package Notes - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Notes tab is used to add a note to the package. The note can include reference information about the package. Notes can be viewed by clicking the Notes tab.

---
The Notes tab is used to add a note to the package. The note can include reference information about the package. Notes can be viewed by clicking the Notes tab.

-   1[Summary](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260604054/Package+Notes#PackageNotes-Summary)
-   2[Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260604054/Package+Notes#PackageNotes-Videos)

## Summary

Company Notes can be entered under Admin > Company > Notes. These Notes can be used to tag assemblies or added as a package note.

To enter a Package Note:

1.  Open a package and click the **Notes** tab.
2.  Click the **New Note** button and click the **Empty** link under the Name field. The Specify Name dialog will display.
3.  **Click the drop-down**.
    1.  If any **Company Notes** have been entered, they will display and can be selected.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260604054/image2019-9-18_10-29-44.png?version=1&modificationDate=1568820585299&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=335&height=250)
    2.  To enter a unique note that will not display in the drop-down, **manually enter the note text** and then **click the note** highlighted in blue.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260604054/image2019-9-18_10-34-39.png?version=1&modificationDate=1568820880503&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    3.  The note will display in the Name field.   
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260604054/image2019-9-18_10-36-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1568820966847&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=762&height=250)
4.  Click the green checkbox to **Save** the package note. Once saved, the User who entered the note and the Date-Time stamp will display.
5.  From any Package's tab, you can see that there is note as the number of notes wil display in the tab.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260604054/image2019-9-18_10-40-27.png?version=1&modificationDate=1568821228819&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=814&height=284)

## Videos

See the Packages Module Overview webinar [**CSG Webinar: STRATUS In-Depth Series, The Packages Module**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#Packages-01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57)) for more information.

# Package Point List - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Stratus supports a web-based workflow for generating Total Station CSV point and DXF graphics files for hanger and other recognized points scoped out using packages.  To use the Point Lists feature the detailer will need to draw the model with points that are designated as Anchor or Positioning points (in Revit), and your Admin will need to setup a Total Station tool and a jobsite station (in Stratus).

---
Stratus supports a web-based workflow for generating Total Station CSV point and DXF graphics files for hanger and other recognized points scoped out using packages.  To use the **Point Lists** feature the detailer will need to draw the model with points that are designated as **Anchor** or **Positioning** points (in Revit), and your Admin will need to setup a Total Station tool and a jobsite station (in Stratus).

Each station in Stratus will correspond to real hardware that you will upload your point lists too. In addition, the package must include hangers for the **Point Lists** > **Generate Point List button** to be enabled.

-   1 [Configure a Total Station Tool and a Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Configure-a-Total-Station-Tool-and-a-Station)
-   2 [Create Points for Point Lists in Revit](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Create-Points-for-Point-Lists-in-Revit)
-   3 [Generate Point Lists in Stratus](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Generate-Point-Lists-in-Stratus)
-   4 [Coordinate System](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Coordinate-System)
-   5 [Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166821968/Package+Point+List#Videos)

**To configure a Total Station Tool and a Station:**

1.  Under Admin > Company > Tools, click **New Tool** and select the **Total Station** Type.
    
2.  Under Admin > Company > Stations, click **New Station**. In this example, the station will be named “Total Station 1”. Select a **Division** that will receive the points on a Total Station. Select the Total Station **tool**.
    

## Create Points for Point Lists in Revit

Points added to a point lists:

-   Point elements (Ex. embedded or nested GTP/Trimble/Evolve point families) must be visible in the source Revit view when published to Stratus.
    
-   _Only get added if they have the correct Point Type._ Point Type is set in your authoring tool. Point Types that get added to point list are **Anchor** or **Positioning**. In the following example, a hanger family type in Revit will be modified to adjust the top point, ensuring it is a Point Type that meets the criteria for inclusion in a point list.
    

1.  In Revit, edit the Revit Family, then edit the sub-part to set the “Point Type” on a hanger:
    
2.  Next select the anchor point:
    
3.  Edit that sub-element (the part that will be the point of interest) and set the Point Type to “Anchor”.
    
4.  After saving this file:
    
    1.  Load the sub family back into the family
        
    2.  Save the family.
        
    3.  Load it back into the model.
        

## Generate Point Lists in Stratus

To Generate Point Lists:

1.  Add the hangers or other parts including points into a package in Stratus under Models > Viewer > Actions > Packages. Points added to the point list are filtered based on point type.
    
2.  Once the package tracking status is locked down by assigning a status that does not allow ‘Can Package’, go into the package details page and open the **Point Lists** tab.  Click the **Generate Point Lists** button.
    
3.  After the point list is generated, make sure the correct Station (Total Station 1) is assigned. Then, click the checkbox for the point list, and then click the **Send Point List to Station** button.
    
4.  Next, click the **Jobsites** menu item and locate the correct station (Total Station 1).  Notice the #Point Lists assigned value is 1 in this example.
    
5.  Once in the Total Station Tool tab you can view the Queued Items and will find the point list from the listed package.  
    
6.  Click the **download** button at the right to **extract the CSV and DXF files** for this point list.  Note: If prompted to allow multiple file downloads, click Yes. The status can be manually updated in this view as well from In Progress to Complete.
    
7.  The resulting points CSV file will look similar to the following:
    
8.  The resulting DXF file will be a subset of the overall model, only containing content within the region of the package definition.  It will display grid lines, centerlines for recognized systems, and point symbols, similar to the following:
    

## Coordinate System

For Revit models that have a shared coordinate transformation, users now have the option to export the CSV and DXF for the Total Station tool using either Shared or Model (Project Internal) coordinates on a per project basis.

To set the Coordinate System:

1.  Under **Admin** > **Project** > **Settings**, select the **Coordinate System** and Save.
    
2.  To export the CSV and DXF files for a point list, see the Configure a Total Station Tool and a Station and   
    Generate Point Lists sections above.
    

## Videos

See the Packages Module Overview webinar [**CSG Webinar: Stratus In-Depth Series, The Packages Module**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#Packages-01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57) "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#Packages-01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57)") for more information.

# Package Properties - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Properties tab is used to review and edit a package's General information, Planning information, and provides a checkbox to archive the package.

---
The Properties tab is used to review and edit a package's General information, Planning information, and provides a checkbox to archive the package.

-   1[General](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-General)
    -   1.1[BIM Area](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-BIMArea)
-   2[Custom Fields](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-CustomFields)
-   3[Package Planning / Actual](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-PackagePlanning%2FActual)
    -   3.1[Planning and Package Creation Summary](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-PlanningandPackageCreationSummary)
    -   3.2[Actual](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-Actual)

## General

The Properties tab is used to review and edit general package information including the package's Name, Number, Description, Package Category, BIM Area, and provides a checkbox to archive the package.  
![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2021-8-9_15-4-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628539455211&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=353)

## BIM Area

1.  Once a package is created the selected BIM Area will display under Packages > Properties > General section. The BIM Area can be edited here.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2021-8-9_13-49-10.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628536664643&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=700&height=388)  
      
    
2.  Click the drop-down. If a new BIM Area is selected, click the **Save** button.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2021-8-9_13-49-59.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628536664823&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=700&height=400)
3.  Notes:
    1.  The BIM Area assignment will **not** update the STRATUS.Part.BIMArea property which is the BIM Area associated with the part.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2021-8-9_15-1-48.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628539309802&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=676&height=230)  
          
        
    2.  The BIM Area assignment will only update the STRATUS.Package.BIMAreaPath property which can be included on a Packages Dashboard report (BIM Area below). **Note**: The STRATUS.Package.BIMAreaPath is editable on the Packages Dashboard.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2021-8-9_15-2-30.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628539351947&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=700&height=387)  
        

## Custom Fields

All available company fields that meet the following criteria will display in the Custom Fields section:

1.  Are associated with packages via a Packages Dashboard report
    
2.  Are set as editable in the company field definition
    
3.  Are not hidden in the report
    
4.  Note: The display name will be the report column header and not the field definition name which is the same as when they appear in the “New Package” dialog.
    

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-1-27_11-22-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1643304178795&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=450&height=571)

## Package Planning / Actual

## Planning and Package Creation Summary

The Planning and Actual section is an optional feature that populates the Start Dates, End Dates, and Durations for Phases on the Packages > Schedule page and reports that reference the STRATUS.Package.\*Duration field.

1.  Initial Phase Duration (days) can be configured:
    1.  At the Company level Company under Admin > Company > Package Categories. See the [**Duration Days Company Level Configuration**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351/Package+Categories+Admin#PackageCategories(Admin)-DurationDays) article for more information. ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-18_15-40-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652906410090&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=333)
    2.  At the Project level under Admin > Projects > Settings. See the [**Duration Days Project Level Configuration**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/217907482/Settings+Project#Settings(Project)-DurationDaysProjectLevelConfiguration) article for more information.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-18_15-39-24.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652906365397&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=469&height=250)
2.  For the Duration Day to be applied to a package during the create package process:  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-18_15-37-20.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652906241948&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=350&height=669)
    1.  **Package Category (required) -** The package category that includes Duration Days for one or more phases must be selected.
    2.  **Phase (optional)** - Phase defaults to **On Site**, but can be changed to a particular Phase. Selecting a phase will only denote which Start Date will be set with the Start Date entered (below). Initial Start Dates will populate the other Phases based on the Duration Days calculations.
    3.  **Start Date (optional)** - The Start Date is used to set the Start Date of the selected Phase.  If a Start Date is not entered, all Phase Start Dates will be empty.
        1.  The meaning of **On Site** is defined by your company.
        2.  On the Packages > Dashboard, the **Required Date = On Site** date.
    4.  **Note: Duration** - If the Package Category selected includes Duration (days), then those Phase Start Dates will be calculated based on the Start Date of the selected Phase (#2).
3.  New Package Creation
    1.  **Phase Start Date** - After the new package is created that includes a Phase Start date, the **Link Phase Calculations** toggle is **off** and users can manually change any individual setting (Ex. Start Date, End Date, or Duration), but this change will not impact other dates or settings. In addition, no date or phase is has the radio button selected to lock the setting.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260603982/image2023-6-23_11-4-59.png?version=1&modificationDate=1687536300568&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  **No Phase Start Date -** After a new package is created that does not include a Phase Start date, the **Link Phase Calculations** button, under the Package’s > Properties > Planning button, will default to On (Enabled) rather than Off (Disabled). This way, when dates are entered in the Planning table, they automatically calculate without having to remember to enable the **Link Phase Calculations** button.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260603982/image2023-9-22_8-18-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1695388684618&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
4.  **Link Phase Calculations** toggle to **on** - Click the **Link Phase Calculations** toggle to **on** when you want to base all phase dates off a date or duration change. For each change made in the Planning table, all of the phase dates will be updated based on that change.  
    **Note:** The **Link Phase Calculations** toggle button can be toggled on or off for each individual user but any updated dates or durations display immediately for all users.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260603982/image2023-6-23_11-5-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1687536353870&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
5.  **Reset Planning Dates** - The **Reset Planning Dates** button is now on the Packages Dashboard making it easier to reset planning dates to the default. This button is still in the Planning table under Properties for each package.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260603982/image2023-6-23_11-7-7.png?version=1&modificationDate=1687536428752&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
6.  **Packages Dashboard** - Editing a package in the Packages Dashboard will adhere to individual package settings for date/duration locks and **Link Phase Calculations**.
7.  Start Date, End Date, and Duration can be edited:
    1.  Under Packages > Schedule by editing the values of the Gantt chart. 
    2.  Under Packages > Properties > Planning in the Planning section (this article).
    3.  Under Packages > Dashboard when a report is configured to use the STRATUS.Package.\*Duration and STRATUS.Package.\*StartDT fields.

Edit Planning Section

A package’s Start Date, End Date, and Duration (days) can be manually edited in the Planning section of the Package’s Properties tab. Any edits will also update the Packages > Schedule after the page has been refreshed. Similarly, any changes to a Phase Start Date, End Date, and Duration (days) on the Packages > Schedule page will also update the Planning section after the page is refreshed.  **Note:** The **On Site** date is not editable under Planning, however, it is editable by editing the Required Date on the Packages Dashboard (Default report).

Only two values are editable at any one time (denoted by the blue circle). Below are the three ways to edit a Phase.

1.  To calculate the End Date:
    1.  Set the Start Date and Duration to be editable.   
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-2-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652554924829&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=863&height=250)
    2.  Change the Duration or Start Date. In this example, the Duration is changed from 2 to 10. 8 week days are added to the End Date which changes from 12/1/2022 to 12/13/2022.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-26-25.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652556387014&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=884&height=250)
2.  To calculate the Duration:
    1.  Set the Start Date and End Date to be editable.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-1-25.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652554887739&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  Change the End Date or Start Date. In this example, the End Date is changed from 12/1/2022 to 12/7/2022. Given the Start Date, the Duration is calculated from 2 days to 6 days.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-25-31.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652556333020&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=838&height=250)
3.  To calculate the Start Date:
    1.  Set the End Date and Duration to be editable.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-20-51.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652556053626&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=850&height=250)
    2.  Change the End Date or Duration. In this example, the End Date is changed from 12/1/2022 to 12/19/2022. Given the Duration, the Start Date is calculated from 11/29/2022 to 12/15/2022.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-14_14-24-26.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652556267103&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=889&height=250)
4.  The Duration (days) Total - Displays the total number of workdays (Saturdays and Sundays) are not included.
5.  Estimated Hours - The Estimated Hours field can be used as needed but is not used in any calculation or report.

## Actual

The Actual data table is read-only and is directly related to the Admin > Company > Tracking Statuses for each Phase (Office, Purchasing, Shop, Field). See the **[Tracking Status (Admin)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761/Tracking+Statuses+Admin)** article for more information.   
![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-16_15-52-1.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652734323120&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=800&height=473)

-   **Start Date** - The Start Date for a Phase displays the date when the package's tracking status was changed to the tracking status associated with 0% for the Phase. All other percentages are ignored for the Actual table. 
-   **End Date** - The End Date for a Phase displays the date when the package's tracking status was changed to the tracking status associated with 100% for the Phase. All other percentages are ignored for the Actual table. 
-   **Duration (days) Total** - The Duration (days) Total displays the total number of workdays (Saturdays and Sundays) are not included.
-   **Install Date** - The Install Date field can be used as needed but is not used in any calculation or report.

Below is an example of the 0% and 100% tracking status associated with each Phase (Office, Purchasing, Shop, Field) under Admin > Company > Tracking Statuses.  
![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/260603982/image2022-5-16_15-12-22.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652910195137&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1200&height=645)
