# Package STRATUS Sheet - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Package's STRATUS Sheet tab displays targeted reports based on details of the selected Package. Some package details like assembly names, spool names, or item numbers can be added to the package before the report is generated. Creating a Package STRATUS Sheet requires a 2-step process: 1) Create a Template and 2) Create a Report associated with the Template.

---
The Package's STRATUS Sheet tab displays targeted reports based on details of the selected Package. Some package details like assembly names, spool names, or item numbers can be added to the package before the report is generated. Creating a Package STRATUS Sheet requires a 2-step process: 1) Create a Template and 2) Create a Report associated with the Template.

-   1 [Packages STRATUS Sheet](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Packages-STRATUS-Sheet)
    -   1.1 [Create a Template](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Create-a-Template)
    -   1.2 [Create a Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Create-a-Report)
    -   1.3 [STRATUS Sheet](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#STRATUS-Sheet)
        -   1.3.1 [PDF](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#PDF)
        -   1.3.2 [Print STRATUS Sheet](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Print-STRATUS-Sheet)
        -   1.3.3 [Full-Screen Mode](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Full-Screen-Mode)
        -   1.3.4 [Pan](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Pan)
        -   1.3.5 [Zoom](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Zoom)
        -   1.3.6 [Extents](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Extents)
        -   1.3.7 [View Orientation and Zoom](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#View-Orientation-and-Zoom)
-   2 [Enabling Higher Resolution Views on STRATUS Sheets](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Enabling-Higher-Resolution-Views-on-STRATUS-Sheets)
    -   2.1 [Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199884912/Package+STRATUS+Sheet#Videos)

## Packages STRATUS Sheet

Creating a Package STRATUS Sheet requires a 2-step process: 1) Create a Template and 2) Create a Report associated with the Template.

## Create a Template

For information on how to create a Template, see the [**Create a Report Template**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974589/Templates+Admin#Templates(Admin)-CreateaReportTemplate.1 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/157974589/Templates+Admin#Templates(Admin)-CreateaReportTemplate.1") article on the Templates (Admin) page.

## Create a Report

For information on how to create a Package Report, see the [**Example: Package Details Report**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393/Reports+Admin#Reports(Admin)-ReportPackageDetailsExample:PackageDetailsReport "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393/Reports+Admin#Reports(Admin)-ReportPackageDetailsExample:PackageDetailsReport") article on the Reports (Admin) page. In order to use the Package's Reports tab, a specifically configured report must be created and associated with a Template. The Report must include the following:

-   **Format** = PDF
    
-   **Item Type** = Package Details 
    
-   **Template** = Any template 
    
-   **Report Fields** = Valid report fields
    

## STRATUS Sheet

### PDF

1.  On the STRATUS Sheet tab, click the **PDF** button.
    
    1.  The PDF will be downloaded to the computer.
        
    2.  The PDF will be opened in a separate browser tab.
        
    3.  The PDF will be added to the Attachments tab.
        
        1.  The file name syntax will be \[Assembly Name\]-\[Report Name\].pdf
            
2.  On an iPad:
    
    1.  Click the **PDF** button. The PDF button text changes to Please Wait.
        
    2.  At the download prompt, click **Download**. 
        
    3.  In Safari, the download icon button displays in the top toolbar while the document is being downloaded. Click this icon to open the file.
        

### Print STRATUS Sheet

The STRATUS Sheet can be printed using the Print button.

1.  Click the **Print** button.
    
2.  Select the printer.
    
3.  If you have an issue printing, see below for browser-specific configurations.
    

### Full-Screen Mode

Click the full-screen mode button to view the STRATUS Sheet in full-screen. To exit full-screen mode, either click the Exit full-screen button or press the Esc key.

### Pan

To pan the STRATUS Sheet, either click the Pan button or press and hold the mouse middle button while panning.

### Zoom

Zoom within a STRATUS Sheet can be accomplished either with the Zoom- and Zoom+ buttons or using the mouse scroll wheel.

### Extents

To return to the default STRATUS Sheet zoom level, click the **Extents** button. 

### View Orientation and Zoom

To specify view orientation and zoom. 

1.  Open a Package's STRATUS Sheet and select the Report. If the package’s orientation has been previously overridden, 2 orientation buttons will display.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/30f81c27-3fa7-40fe-9924-73ac82f8dc7c)
    
2.  **Reset viewer orientation for this package** 
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/6839128e-bd54-46d0-b5b1-61c44d82df2a)
    
    \- Click this to restore the package’s original orientation and zoom.
3.  **Set viewer orientation and zoom as default image for view for this package**
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/a652cc56-6a7d-444a-963c-b991dd2d9cac)
    
     **-** Click this to set the default viewer orientation for this package. The page view will change focusing your actions on orienting and zooming the package in the viewer and then clicking the **Save Orientation** button. The **Fit To View** button is like pressing the “F” key to Fit to the view. **Note**: This will be the only button to display if the original default orientation is the current view.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/0debe10f-8586-41b8-87ae-19b82eeac0af)
    
4.  Once **Save Orientation** is clicked, the Package’s Viewer will refresh, and the new default orientation will display.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/7c5e08ad-c8b0-4132-9485-ffca0d0b0cb4)
    
    1.  **Attachments tab notes:** The selected report's STRATUS Sheet saved isometric view can also be displayed in a report on the Package's > Attachments tab. Here, the report can either be selected, or the report can be included as a sub-report of a Master report. In either case, the report content will display the isometric view as saved in the Package's STRATUS Sheet.
        

## Enabling Higher Resolution Views on STRATUS Sheets

There is a hidden setting we have that controls the resolution of this output.  We had some browsers incapable of rendering higher resolution quality and therefore set the default value rather low to ensure success for all users.  We have noticed some of you like to generate some larger sheets where having higher resolution 3D view images might be nice. Here is how to change the setting by simply modifying a value in your web browser. 

1.  In Chrome, I press F12 to open Developer tools, or you can access it from the menu as shown here (other browsers will have a similar option). 
    
2.  Once the Developer tools window is opened, find the ‘Application’ tab, then Storage \\ Local Storage \\ https://www.gtpstratus.com and type **gtp-stratus-max** into the filter or just sort by Key value and locate the entry.
    
3.  You can assign a larger value to the **gtp-stratus-max-webgl-canvas-width-height**, such as 10000 which is as high as we have tested.  If you start getting black boxes where the 3D views are, the value is too large.
    

## Videos

See the Packages Module Overview webinar [**CSG Webinar: STRATUS In-Depth Series, The Packages Module**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57) "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57)") for more information.

# Package Tasks - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Task items are the instances of company defined task definitions, which belong to task workflows optionally assigned to assemblies and parts. Each task item knows the assembly or part to which it belongs and holds a reference to the user and/or station with start and completed time stamps. The Tasks tab can display a tasks Kanban board (To Do, In Progress, Done) for each package.  The task workflow is configured at the company level and enables a company to apply a task sequence to an order.

---
Task items are the instances of company defined task definitions, which belong to task workflows optionally assigned to assemblies and parts. Each task item knows the assembly or part to which it belongs and holds a reference to the user and/or station with start and completed time stamps. The Tasks tab can display a tasks Kanban board (To Do, In Progress, Done) for each package.  The task workflow is configured at the company level and enables a company to apply a task sequence to an order. 

-   1[Configure a Task Workflow](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170688627/Package+Tasks#PackageTasks-ConfigureaTaskWorkflow)
-   2[Assign a Task Workflow to Items](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170688627/Package+Tasks#PackageTasks-AssignaTaskWorkflowtoItems)
-   3[Generate Tasks](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/170688627/Package+Tasks#PackageTasks-GenerateTasks)

## Configure a Task Workflow

1.  **Task Categories** - Enter how your company wants to categorize tasks under **Admin > Task Categories**. Task Categories which are used to categorize Task Definitions like Bending, Cutting, Detailing, Installing, etc.  Below is an example. 
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/170688627/image2018-8-23_14-42-56.png?version=1&modificationDate=1535053378608&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=890&height=376)
    
2.  **Task Definitions** - Enter your company's Task Definitions under the **Admin > Task Definitions**.  Task Definitions are process tasks. You can make them as detailed or broad as you like.  Below is an example.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/170688627/image2018-8-23_14-50-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1535053820030&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=901&height=321)
    
3.  **Configure your Task Workflows**. A task workflow is a sequence of tasks.  When tasks are generated under the package's **Tasks tab**, each task under Task Sequence will be assigned to part, assembly, or package and will display on a Kanban board.
    1.  **Name and Description** - Enter a task workflow name and description.
    2.  **Apply to Type** - Apply it to a type (part, assembly or package). Task workflows are assigned on the package's **Items tab** and each item in the package is identified as a part, assembly, or package. This setting helps filter the list so you won't be able to apply a task workflow to an assembly that is targeted to a part.
    3.  **Cost Category** - Set the Cost Category.
    4.  **Task Sequence** - Select tasks to be done for each item and then order them as needed. These tasks are defined under Task Definitions. Below is an example.
        
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/170688627/image2018-8-23_15-0-19.png?version=1&modificationDate=1535054421159&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=953&height=364)
        
4.  You are ready to assign tasks under the package's **Items tab**.

## Assign a Task Workflow to Items

1.  Click the **Items tab** which lists the items (parts and assemblies) that are included in the package.
2.  Assign each item to a Task Workflow. You can select multiple item checboxes and then select a Task Workflow for one of the checked items and all checked items will be set. Below is an example.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/170688627/image2019-10-7_8-55-47.png?version=1&modificationDate=1570456549110&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=755&height=250)
    

## Generate Tasks

1.  After you have assigned a Task Workflow to all the items, make sure the package tracking status has changed to a non-Can Package status.
2.  Click the **Task tab**. The Generate Tasks button will be enabled.
3.  Click the **Generate Tasks** button and the task will be created on the Kanban board.

**Task Color**

The task color comes from the Admin > Company > Task Category where each task category is associated with a color.  On the Admin > Company > Task Definitions page, a Task Category is assigned to a Task Definition. And then finally, on the Admin > Company > Task Workflow page, you assign tasks in the Task Sequence area which are associated with the Task Definitions.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/170688627/image2024-2-23_12-37-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1708713473184&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

# Package Tracking - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Package's Tracking tab is one place to change the tracking status of a package. Your company administrator can turn on/off options for each tracking status.

---
## Package Tracking

The Package's Tracking tab is one place to change the tracking status of a package. Your company administrator can turn on/off options for each tracking status.

-   1 [Tracking Tab](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/201719920/Package+Tracking#Tracking-Tab)

## Tracking Tab

1.  When a new package is created, it is assigned with the first Tracking Status in your company's list under Admin > Company > Tracking Statuses whose **Can Package** checkbox is checked.
    
2.  Once a package is opened and the Tracking tab clicked, the tracking status log for the package will display.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/f19e5d9a-9fdb-465f-b575-47c23194f88a#media-blob-url=true&id=514ea9ed-240c-4a76-890f-367b663ae321&collection=contentId-201719920&contextId=201719920&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image2022-5-25_15-13-52.png&size=82333&width=1286&height=409&alt=)
    
    1.  **CSV | Excel** - The exported Tracking table fields include the following:  
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4aa3f7f4-407f-490c-8f2f-55349931887a)
        
    2.  **User** - The name of the user who applied the tracking status change.
        
    3.  **Date-Time** - The Date-Time the tracking status change was applied.
        
    4.  **Status** - The tracking Status and tracking Status color applied when the tracking Status was updated.
        
    5.  **Comment** - Comments are added in a variety of ways:
        
        ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d8f15f24-87c5-40e6-9b53-638ef9fa1738#media-blob-url=true&id=369c5200-5887-4033-8845-8f904640ebe2&collection=contentId-201719920&contextId=201719920&mimeType=image%2Fpng&name=image2023-9-20_10-0-10.png&size=55859&width=935&height=409&alt=)
        
        1.  **Automatically by Stratus.**
            
            1.  Package Creation
                
                1.  Comment = Publish
                    
            2.  Package added to Container
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Added to \[Container Name\] 
                    
            3.  Package removed from Container
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Removed from \[Container Name\] 
                    
            4.  Tracking Status comment made to an Assembly contained within the Package
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Automated Event 
                    
            5.  Downgrade a Part Tracking Status on a Package which forces the whole Package to downgrade
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Automated Event
                    
            6.  Updates during the import/publish process for packages/assemblies/parts
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Automated Event
                    
            7.  Adding an assembly to a package
                
                1.  Comment = Stratus Automated Event
                    
            8.  Downgrade an Assembly Tracking Status belonging to a Package
                
                1.  Automated Event - Part Tracking Status Update \[Tracking Status Name\].
                    
        2.  **Manually by User**
            
            1.  In the Comments column under Packages > Viewer > Tracking table.
                
            2.  In the comment field of an API POST.
                
            3.  In the Comment textbox on any Package > Viewer page. Click the **Apply** button to make the change.
                
                ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/90c10582-c1ea-4f5c-8517-4b219c25a2e8)
                
    6.  **Division** - The Division selected an applied by the user.
        
    7.  **Hours** - The Hours entered an applied by the user.
        
    8.  **Attachments** - Users can attach a file to the assembly. See the [**File Attachment Workflow**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/File+Attachment+Workflow "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/File+Attachment+Workflow") article for more information.
        
    9.  **Remove Selected Item** - Deletes the associated tracking row.
        
3.  To change the tracking status, a user can either:
    
    1.  Click the **Next Tracking Status** button and then click **Apply**.
        
        ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/c23f64c7-8543-4c34-b065-0a0cd8a57cbf/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-201719920&height=109&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMDE3MTk5MjAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY3MjkxLCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjQ0MTF9.WEkvpUCLgxXZST40FQoJaN8PfeHfaM3_rhqOnvMbZfg&width=838)
        
        1.  **When Same Part in Multiple Packages Note:**  When packages have different package categories but include the same parts, the status changes will affect both packages. For example:
            
            1.  Packages Name Multi 1 and Multi 2 have same parts. One Package has the Default category and the other Fabrication Production.
                
                ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/cb11367d-7ee8-428e-85d5-7cc8075aa621/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-201719920&height=223&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMDE3MTk5MjAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY3MjkxLCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjQ0MTF9.WEkvpUCLgxXZST40FQoJaN8PfeHfaM3_rhqOnvMbZfg&width=830)
                
            2.  Click on Package Number 123-2022-0084, click Tracking and then change the Status to Spooled.
                
                ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/9960aff6-9cb7-4559-a1b7-b6996054192b)
                
            3.  On the Packages > Dashboard, both Packages are now updated to the same Spooled Status.
                
                ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/953373bd-c197-4287-bf53-e50751dd3303)
                
    2.  Click the **Status selector drop-down**, select a **status**, and then click **Apply**.
        
        ![](https://media-cdn.atlassian.com/file/e206a43d-1878-4a62-9807-c9c8377aa248/image/cdn?allowAnimated=true&client=5f4a70b1-9d9d-47c3-b388-87235680bb54&collection=contentId-201719920&height=363&max-age=2592000&mode=full-fit&source=mediaCard&token=eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiJ9.eyJpc3MiOiI1ZjRhNzBiMS05ZDlkLTQ3YzMtYjM4OC04NzIzNTY4MGJiNTQiLCJhY2Nlc3MiOnsidXJuOmZpbGVzdG9yZTpjb2xsZWN0aW9uOmNvbnRlbnRJZC0yMDE3MTk5MjAiOlsicmVhZCJdfSwiZXhwIjoxNzUwODY3MjkxLCJuYmYiOjE3NTA4NjQ0MTF9.WEkvpUCLgxXZST40FQoJaN8PfeHfaM3_rhqOnvMbZfg&width=886)
        
4.  Deleting tracking entries from the log for a package or assembly requires the button to be clicked by either the user who originally created the tracking entry or a project admin.

# Packages - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Packages tab is a hub from which the package workflow can be managed. Depending on your company, a STRATUS package is also also known as an order, shop ticket, or work package. From the Package tab you can access the Dashboard, Schedule, and Status Board that includes packages for all projects. To view the detail of a specific package, click the package name for tabs that include Properties, Items, Tasks, Cut Lists, Viewer, Attachments, and Tracking.

---
The Packages tab is a hub from which the package workflow can be managed. Depending on your company, a STRATUS package is also also known as an order, shop ticket, or work package. From the Package tab you can access the Dashboard, Schedule, and Status Board that includes packages for all projects. To view the detail of a specific package, click the package name for tabs that include Properties, Items, Tasks, Cut Lists, Viewer, Attachments, and Tracking.

# Packages Dashboard - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Packages Dashboard is a filtered list of project packages that can be sorted, filtered, edited, and some columns can be totaled.  A "Default" report includes summary details described below, but you can create your own report(s) to display the data, calculated fields, editable fields needed for your company. The Default report provides the ability to open and delete packages, set the Required date for each package, change the package Status, open package attachments, and create .MAJ or .PCF file attachments. Note: For correct dates, verify that your computer's time zone is correct.

---
The Packages Dashboard is a filtered list of project packages that can be sorted, filtered, edited, and some columns can be totaled.  A "Default" report includes summary details described below, but you can create your own report(s) to display the data, calculated fields, editable fields needed for your company. The Default report provides the ability to open and delete packages, set the Required date for each package, change the package Status, open package attachments, and create .MAJ or .PCF file attachments. Note: For correct dates, verify that your computer's time zone is correct.

-   1 [Default Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Default-Report)
    -   1.1 [Columns](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Columns)
    -   1.2 [Filter and Sort the Dashboard](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Filter-and-Sort-the-Dashboard)
        -   1.2.1 [Filters](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Filters)
        -   1.2.2 [Date Window Filter](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Date-Window-Filter)

## Default Report

The Default report is available out-of-the-box. Custom reports can be created and will display in the Report drop-down. See the Package Dashboard Reports example in the [**Reports (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393") article for more information.

## Columns

1.  **Package Number** and **Package Name** \- Open a package by clicking the Package Number or Package Name link. Opening the package will display the package tabs that enable you to work with the package (Ex. Viewer, Cut Lists, Tasks, etc.). The Package Number and Package Name were assigned to the package when it was created and can be edited by opening the package, clicking the Properties tab, and then editing the Name or Number fields. The Package Description, Category, Estimated Hours, Start Date, and Required Date can also be edited in the Properties tab for the package. A Package is created in the:
    
    1.  Models > Viewer page
        
    2.  Projects > Deliverables page
        
    3.  Packages Dashboard page when the **New Package** is used
        
2.  **Model** \- The name and link to the model from which the package was created.
    
3.  **Description** \- The Description of the package if entered.
    
4.  **Required** \- The Required date on the Default report, if known, is the date that the package materials are required to be on-site for the Field Phase Start Date. The Required date can be edited in-grid, or on the [**Package Properties**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982") tab, or on the [**Packages Schedule**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9044061 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9044061").
    
5.  **\# Assemblies** - The number of assemblies in the package.
    
6.  **\# Parts** \- The number of loose parts (not found in assemblies) in the package.
    
7.  **\# Total Parts** - The total number of parts including loose parts and those in assemblies.
    
8.  **\# Tasks** - If a Task Workflow has been applied to a package, the # Tasks indicates the number of tasks that have been created for the package. See the [**Task Definitions (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/240713729 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/240713729") article for more information.
    
9.  **% Complete** - % Complete is calculated differently depending on whether the package includes tasks or not.
    
    1.  **Package includes tasks** - When a package has tasks associated with its child assemblies or parts, the completeness of the tasks is used to calculate the % complete for the package.
        
    2.  **Package does not include tasks** - When the package does not have tasks, the % Complete calculation is based on the packages' tracking status percentages. See the [**Tracking Statuses (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761") article for information about how to setup % complete values.
        
10.  **Hours** **Estimated** \- Estimate Hours are manually entered when the package is created, except when the package is created from the Projects > Deliverables page. Estimated Hours can be edited in-grid. The editable Estimated Hours field uses the **STRATUS.Package.HoursEstimatedShop** property in both default and custom reports.
    
11.  **Actual Hours** - Actual Hours are manually entered when the package Tracking Status changes and the Update Tracking Status dialog displays. Actual Hours can be applied to a Part, Assembly, or Package and the tracking log hours now bubble up to the package level. For example:
    
    **If a part and assembly belong to a package and actual hours are entered:**
    
    Part = 1; Part = 1.5; Part = 3; Part = -2  
    Assembly = 5; Assembly = 7  
    Package = 10  
    Packages Dashboard = 35.5
    
    **If part and assembly are in two different Package Categories and actual hours are entered:**
    
    Part = 1; Part = 1.5; Part = 3; Part = -2  
    Assembly = 5; Assembly = 7  
    Package = 10  
    Packages Dashboard for both packages = 35.5
    
12.  **Division** - The Division can be entered when the package Tracking Status changes and the Update Tracking Status dialog displays. The Division can be edited in-grid.
    
    1.  The default settings for Division when creating a New Package, under Packages Dashboard and clicking the New Package button, will be the user’s last setting for Division.
        
13.  **Status** - The Tracking Status can be changed (in-grid) by clicking the Status link which will display the Update Tracking Status dialog.
    
    1.  The default settings when creating a New Package, under Packages Dashboard and clicking the **New Package** button, will be the user’s last setting for Status.
        
14.  **Job**
    
    1.  If a MAJ or PCF file has been generated, the Job column will display.
        
    2.  A download button and create date will display if a .MAJ has been generated.
        
    3.  Click the download icon and your web browser will prompt you to save the file. A .MAJ file contains both fabricated and non-fabricated items that are part of the package.
        
15.  **Attachments**
    
    1.  The **Upload Attachment** button can be used to locate and upload attachments to any package on the Packages Dashboard. See the [**Add Attachment**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Add-Attachment "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Add-Attachment") section in Attachments article for more information.
        
    2.  Clicking the **Open Attachment** button will display the attachment fly-out.
        
    3.  See the [**Dashboard Attachments**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Dashboard-Attachments "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969/Attachments#Dashboard-Attachments") section in Attachments article for more information on previewing the attachment, downloading a single attachment, downloading All attachments or downloading a ZIP of all attachments.
        
16.  **Actions**
    
    1.  **MAJ / PCF**
        
        1.  For published Fabrication drawings, click either the **MAJ** button to generate a MAJ file, or the **PCF** button to generate a PCF file.
            
        2.  Once the file has generated, it will display in the **Job** column and under the **Open Attachment** button fly-out where the file can be dowloaded.
            
        3.  **Note**: If you receive an error attempting to generate an output file, see the [**Fabrication Job issue creating MAJ or PCF files from the Packages Dashboard**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/246153241 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/246153241") article.
            
        4.  For information on automatically generating a .MAJ see the [**Generate Automated .MAJ CamDuct Cut List File**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746#PackageCutLists-Automated.1 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746#PackageCutLists-Automated.1") article.
            
        5.  For information on automatically generating a .PCF file, see the [**Generate Automated .PCF PypeServer Cut List File**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746#PackageCutLists-Automated "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166723746#PackageCutLists-Automated") article.
            
        6.  Custom Data Fields - STRATUS custom data fields can be included in a .MAJ file.
            
            1.  A custom data field is published and edited.
                
            2.  A MAJ file can be generated and opened with edited custom field on parts:
                
    2.  **Reset Planning Dates** - Click the **Reset Planning Dates** button to reset all planning dates to their default values.
        
    3.  **Toggle Archive Status** \- Use the Toggle Archive Status to archive selected packages. By default, the Toggle Archive Status button will only be permissioned (visible) to users who have the Project Admin role. When clicked, the **Toggle Package Archive Status** prompt will display.
        
    4.  **Delete** - Click the **Delete** button to delete the package. All parts and assemblies will be disassociated from the package.
        
17.  **Totals** - By default, numeric columns (Integer and Decimal which includes # Assemblies, # Parts, # Total Parts, Tasks, Estimated Hours, and Actual Hours) are totaled. In addition, Feet Inch totals can be added to a custom report by configuring the report’s Total Values setting to Yes for the target columns. See the Package Dashboard Reports example in the [**Reports (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393") article for more information. 
    
    1.  All Dashboard pages that have more than one page of data will include 2 totals. In this case a subtotal (150.29’) for the packages on the page, followed by the total for all packages (24226.2’) defined by the Project and Model selected.
        

## Filter and Sort the Dashboard

### Filters

**Filter the dashboard by one or more of the following:**

-   Filter by one Project or All Projects.
    
-   Filter by one Model or All Models.
    
-   Filter by one or more Divisions (defaults to ALL Divisions).
    
-   Filter by one or more Statuses (defaults to ALL Statuses).
    
-   Filter by one or more company package Categories (defaults to ALL Categories).
    
-   Filter by using the **Search** option which searches the package by name, number, model, required, Division, or tracking status. In addition, if search criteria is entered while the Packages Dashboard is loading, any packages matching the criteria will immediately display at the top of the table.
    
-   Filter the dashboard content by clicking a **Filters** button in the column header, then click the filters arrow that displays, and then select use the selection interface to filter the list. See the [**How does the column filter work?**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/452919459/Sort+and+Filter+Data+Tables#How-does-the-column-filter-work%3F "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/452919459/Sort+and+Filter+Data+Tables#How-does-the-column-filter-work%3F") article for more information.
    

When a filter criteria finds no results the following message will display:

1.  Assemblies > Dashboard
    
2.  Packages > Dashboard
    

To filter to packages that do not have a Required Date:

1.  Click the **Filter** button. A filter will display.
    
2.  Click the red x for both fields. Empty Required Dates will display.
    

### Date Window Filter

When enabled the date window filter will filter the dashboard data table to items whose date is a specified number of days before and after the current date. This tool is targeted at those who prefer to view packages within a consistent date range window every time the page is loaded. These settings will persist on the Packages Dashboard, Schedule, and Status Board until they are changed on any page or turned off.

**To use the Date Window filter:**

1.  The Date Window filter is off by default.
    
2.  Click the Date Window filter button to display the dialog.
    
3.  Click the gear icon to display configuration options.
    
    1.  **Include empty dates**
        
        1.  **Checked** - When checked if an item’s date field is Empty, it will display in the data table.
            
        2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked if an item’s date field is Empty, it will not display in the data table.
            
    2.  **Count Days as**
        
        1.  **Business** - For the business day calculation, weekends are excluded while public holidays are included as a business day.
            
        2.  **Calendar** - For the calendar day calculation, all days are included.
            
4.  To configure the date window:
    
    1.  **Date drop-down** - The Date drop-down displays all planning date fields located under Packages > Properties > Planning. **Note**: The Default is the Required date which also displays on the Packages > Dashboard default report. Select one date field.
        
    2.  To select the number of days prior to today, click the number and either enter a number or use the up/down arrow to change the value. The exact date the number references will display (hover text) as the number value changes. In this example, 10 days (business days) prior to today is 6/7/2022.
        
    3.  To select the number of days after today, click the number and either enter a number or use the up/down arrow to change the value. The exact date the number references will display (hover text) as the number value changes. In this example, 15 days (business days) after today is 7/12/2022.
        
5.  When done, the data table will filter to display only items that meet the criteria. Once set, these settings will continue to be used until they are changed.
    

### Sort

Users can manually sort a column heading by clicking the **Sort** button which will override the existing primary sort. See the [**Sort and Filter Data Tables**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/452919459 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/452919459") FAQ for more information.

-   **Click Sort button** - Any sort button has 3 states:
    
    -   **Click 1** - sorts the column in ascending order.
        
    -   **Click 2** - sorts the column in descending order.
        
    -   **Click 3** - sets the table back to the default sort order according to either the pre-defined table sort order (if one exists) or the sort order specified by the report’s sort index settings.
        
-   **Default Reports** - Default reports for the following dashboards include a default sort order. After a user manually changes the sort order for a dashboard, that sort order will override the default sort order and will continue to be the primary sort on that table for that user until the user changes it.
    
    -   **Packages Dashboard** \- Required date
        
    -   **Assemblies Dashboard** - Assembly Name
        
    -   **Container Dashboard**
        
        -   **Report** \- Container Type
            
        -   **Details Report** - Item Type
            
-   **Custom Reports (Sort Index)** - Report designers can specify a Sort Index for custom reports under Admin > Company > Reports > Report Fields. When a custom report is first loaded by a user, the Sort Index with the lowest number will be the primary sort. The next lowest index number will be a secondary sort when the primary sort includes identical values. Ex. If the table displays states, cities, and zip codes where state is sort index 1, city is sort index 2, and zip code is sort index 3, then, the primary sort will be state, the secondary sort will be cities which will be sorted alphabetically, and zip codes will be the third sort when there is more than one city.
    
    -   **Note**: After a user manually changes the sort order for a dashboard, that sort order will override the default sort order and will continue to be the primary sort on that table for that user until the user changes it. The lowest sort index will become the secondary sort, and so on.
        
-   **Reset Sorting** - Another way to sets the table back to the default sort order is to click the **Reset sorting** button.
    

## Display Active or Archived Packages

Once archived:

1.  The package will not display on the Packages Dashboard unless the Archived tab is selected. Use the Status "Active" or "Archived" filter in the Package dashboard.
    
2.  If an archived package is opened, only the Properties tab will display and all Properties will be disabled, except the ability to uncheck the Archived option.
    
3.  An archived package will display in the Models > Viewer under **Display Modes** and **Filters** where the Archived lable displays along with a hyperlink to the Package’s Properties page.
    
4.  Also on the Models > Viewer, with the **Actions > Packages** panel open, when an archived package is clicked it will display the **Archived** label and include a link to the package.
    

## Cached Calculated Values

Calculated field values are automatically cached and purged for each package. Package Dashboard cached values are automatically purged when:

-   any type of update changes values, such as editing parts in a package or assembly
    
-   using a field that is a total value from all parts in the package
    
-   a Field references a Part property, or another Field value and they are modified
    

**Clear Cached Calculated Field Values and Reload Data Table**

The **Clear Cached Calculated Field Values and Reload Data Table** button forces calculated values to be refreshed. This button should only be needed as a backup as the Packages Dashboard will detect when calculated fields need to be refreshed.

## Paging

The Packages Dashboard uses Paging to load the data table. When the Packages Dashboard initially loads, all Package Names and non-calculated fields will load first. Calculated data will continue to load and replace skeleton placeholders on the dashboard until all data is populated. The benefit is that while data is populating, functions like sorting, filtering, package links, generate MAJ, update Status, and edit fields are available. When a non-calculated column is used as a filter, packages at the top of the newly filtered dashboard will begin to load. Totals will continue to update as row values are calculated. The data table loading indicator (red bar) will display until all data displays in the data table.

## New Package

The New Package button is primarily used for non-modeled Field Requests. By creating a package and then attaching a sketch or document to the package, the normal package workflow can be used to track the package and assembly through the project. See the [**Field Requests**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/242974730 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/242974730") article for more information.

## New Package Prerequisites

Before creating a New Package when the "Add Assemblies and Parts" checkbox is checked, verify the following in the Models > Viewer. If unchecked, the prerequisites can be ignored.

1.  **Company Filter** – Verify that the Company filter that will be selected works.
    
2.  **Package Category** – Verify that the parts being added to the package are not already included in the same package category. **Note:** If any part/assembly is already included in the selected Package Category, the part/assembly will not be added to the package and you will not receive a confirmation notification.  See the [**Package Categories (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351") article for more information.
    
3.  **Tracking Status** – Verify that the filtered parts are in a "Can Package" tracking status. See the [**Tracking Statuses (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10485761") article for more information.
    
4.  **Area** – Verify that the target Area is included under Admin > Projects > Areas.  See the [**Areas (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/103284742 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/103284742") article for more information.
    

## Create New Package

To create a new package from the Packages Dashboard:

1.  Click the **New Package** button. The New Package dialog will display.
    
    1.  **Category** - Select the **Package Category**. In this example, the resulting package will be hangers for a specific area and the selected Package Category does not include assemblies. As a result, if these hangers are part of an assembly, the assemblies will not be included in the package.  See the [**Package Categories (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/166199351") article for more information.  **Note:** If any part/assembly is already included in the selected Package Category, the part/assembly will not be added to the package and you will not receive a confirmation notification.
        
    2.  **Number** \- When creating a Package in the Packages Dashboard, the default **Number** is derived from the Naming Convention configured by the Admin.
        
        1.  If the Package Name Naming Convention refers to information that does not require a part be selected (Ex. Date, Project Number) then those will automatically populate the **Number**. See the [**Naming and Numbering (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/164134913 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/164134913") article for more information. 
            
        2.  If the Package Name Naming Convention refers to information where a part must be selected (Ex. BIM Area Abbreviation or System/Service), then you will need to manually enter the data now or at a later time.
            
        3.  **Incrementor Checkbox** \- The Incrementor checkbox can be used to ensure the number is unique. It is not required that Package Number be unique.
            
    3.  **Name** - When creating a Package in the Packages Dashboard, the default **Name** is derived from the Naming Convention configured by the Admin.
        
        1.  If the Package Name Naming Convention refers to information that does not require a part be selected (Ex. Date, Project Number) then those will automatically populate the **Name**. See the [**Naming and Numbering (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/164134913 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/164134913") article for more information. 
            
        2.  If the Package Name Naming Convention refers to information where a part must be selected (Ex. BIM Area Abbreviation or System/Service), then you will need to manually enter the data now or at a later time.
            
        3.  **Incrementor Checkbox** \- The Incrementor checkbox can be used to ensure the number is unique. It is required that Package Name be unique.
            
    4.  **Status** – Set the **Tracking Status** the package will be in once created.
        
    5.  **Division** - Set the package **Division** (if any) once it is created.
        
    6.  **Description** – Include a **Description** to clarify the package if needed.
        
    7.  **Phase** – Phase defaults to **Required Date**. Enter a **Required Date** to communicate with the project manager and shop.
        
    8.  **Add Assemblies and Parts** checkbox - Check the **Add Assemblies and Parts** checkbox to automatically add parts/assemblies that meet the Filter and Area selections below.
        
        1.  **Filter** – Select the single **Filter** to be used to isolate the parts/assemblies. See the [**Filters (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617224 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617224") article for more information. **Note**: Validate that the filter works in the model.
            
        2.  **Area** – Select the single **Area** the package will include. See the [**Areas (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/103284742 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/103284742") article for more information. Below is an example of the Areas drop-down list. **Note**: Validate that the area works in the model.
            
    9.  **Estimating Information** - The **Estimating Information** data cannot be edited until parts are added to the package.
        
    10.  **Additional Fields** - The **Additional Fields** data cannot be edited until parts are added to the package.
        
2.  Click the **Create Package** button and the package will display on the Packages Dashboard and will include any entered Data and the number of Parts and Total Parts that were added to the package. No assemblies were added since the selected Package Category ignored assemblies.
    

## Download CSV or Excel

The Packages Dashboard for a project and model can be downloaded to a CSV file or an Excel file.

## Import CSV

A CSV file can be imported to either create new packages or update existing packages. This feature could be used in various scheduling scenarios where packages with start dates and other fields could be imported into STRATUS from a Project Scheduling tool that can output to CSV format.

**Note**: When importing a file back into STRATUS: 1) only a CSV file can be imported back into STRATUS, and 2) the Package Dashboard must be filtered to one project and one model for the **Import CSV** button to be enabled.

### File Configuration

A CSV file that will be imported using the Import CSV button can be created in several different ways. In the examples below, the 2 packages already exist.

**To Configure the file Format and Field Values**

1.  Create a file in one of two ways:
    
    1.  **Create a new file** \- Create a new file with the required field headers and then add any optional fields below.
        
        1.  **Package Number (Required)**
            
        2.  **Package Name (Required)**
            
        3.  **Id (Required)** - This field is required to be in the file, but should be left blank for new rows.
            
        4.  With only the required fields a comma-delimited CSV file might look like this where row 2 is a package that will be imported.
            
    2.  **Download an Existing CSV File or Excel File** \- Click the **CSV** or **Excel** button. The file will download the field headers and data associated with the selected Packages Dashboard Report. In the example below, the **Default** report was selected and includes 4 rows of data.
        
        1.  Open the File in Excel. The following fields display.
            
        2.  Open the File in Notepad or Notepad++. The following fields display.
            
2.  **Optional Fields**  
    The following optional fields can be added to the file. Optional fields that include data will update the package during the Import CSV process. Fields that do not include data will be ignored. The Field header name used in the CSV file will depend on the report format specified in the package dashboard, otherwise the STRATUS.Package.\* name will always work. See the Header section of the [**Report Fields**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393#Reports(Admin)-ReportFields "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/10617393#Reports(Admin)-ReportFields") topic for more information.
    
    1.  **Description** \- The Description field is optional.
        
    2.  **STRATUS.Package.StartDT** \- The STRATUS.Package.StartDT will only be updated if it is a valid date-time value (Ex. 03/24/21).
        
    3.  **STRATUS.Package.Required or the Header name specified in the report format** \- The RequiredDT will only be updated if it is a valid date-time value (Ex. 03/24/21).
        
    4.  **STRATUS.Package.HoursEstimatedShop or the Header name specified in the report format** \- The HoursEstimated value must be a valid number or will be set to zero.
        
    5.  **STRATUS.Field.\*** **or the Header name specified in the report format** \- Any STRATUS.Field.\* value that is editable can be updated. Note: If the editable field is defined as a date-time format, a valid date-time value must be entered (Ex. 03/24/21).
        
    6.  **STRATUS.Package.CategoryName** \- If the STRATUS.Package.CategoryName field is not included, the Package Category named Default will be applied to new imported packages. **Note**: In this scenario, a Package Category named Default must exist. Out-of-the-box the Default Package Category does exist but it can be deleted or renamed.
        
    7.  **STRATUS.Package.Notes**
        
        1.  **Existing Notes** - Existing Notes will not be removed.
            
        2.  **Duplicate Note** - If a duplicate Note is found, the newest Note will not be added to the Packages Dashboard during the Import process.
            
        3.  **Multiple Notes** - Multiple Notes should be entered using a semicolon as a separator between notes.
            
3.  **Ignored Fields**  
    The following fields will always be ignored by the Import CSV process and will never be used to update a package.
    
    1.  **Model**
        
    2.  **#Assemblies**
        
    3.  **#Parts**
        
    4.  **#Total Parts**
        
    5.  **#Tasks**
        
    6.  **%Complete**
        
    7.  **Actual Hours**
        
    8.  **Division**
        
    9.  **Status (Active or Archived)**
        
    10.  **Tracking Status** \- Like other new packages, any new package included in the import file will be assigned the first available “Applies to Package” tracking status.
        
    11.  **Category** \- Category data is only used when constructing NEW packages, cannot modify this property.
        
    12.  **Category Abbreviation** - Category Abbreviation data is only used when constructing NEW packages, cannot modify this property.
        

### Import Process

For this example, to import a CSV file with one new package the following CSV file will be used. For additional packages, add rows to the file. The CSV file can be imported many times and only the new or updated information will be imported.

1.  If an Excel file was used to edit field values in the previous section, save the file as a CSV file format.
    
2.  **Enable / Disable Import CSV button** - On the Packages Dashboard, the **Import CSV** button will remain disabled until one project and one model have been selected. Neither ALL PROJECTS nor ALL MODELS can be selected.
    
3.  Click the **Import CSV** button.
    
4.  The Import Packages dialog will display. Click the **Browse** button and locate the CSV file.
    
5.  The Upload Packages CSV File dialog will display. Click the **Upload** button.
    
6.  Once the file has uploaded the Close button will be active. Click the **Close** button.
    
7.  The Import packages dialog will display again, this time with the CSV file ready to be imported. Click the **Import** button.
    
8.  Once the file has imported, the following message will display. Click the **OK** button.
    
9.  After the Packages Dashboard refreshes:
    
    1.  **Packages Dashboard -** The new package will display on the Packages Dashboard. Some of the data entered in the CSV file are highlighted on this page.
        
    2.  **Package’s Properties** - The STRATUS.Package.StartDT and STRATUS.Package.CategoryName fields display on the Package’s Properties tab along with the other CSV field data.
        
    3.  **Package’s Notes** \- The STRATUS.Package.Notes field displays on the Package’s Notes tab.
        
10.  **Note:** Like all packages, when a package is created via the Import CSV process, it will:
    
    1.  Display as an Activity under Admin > Company > Activities.
        
    2.  Display as a Notification.

# Packages Schedule - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Packages Schedule tab works in conjunction with the Packages > Package Planning / Actual feature.

---
The Packages Schedule tab works in conjunction with the Packages > [**Package Planning / Actual**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/260603982/Package+Properties#PackageProperties-PackagePlanning%2FActual) feature.

-   **Project Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Projects.
    
-   **Model Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Models.
    
-   **Division Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Divisions.
-   **Category Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Categories.
-   **Phase Filter** \- Filter list of packages by Phase including Office, Purchasing, Shop, and Field.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2022-8-3_10-30-57.png?version=1&modificationDate=1659540658602&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=824&height=250)
    
-   **Date Window Filter** - When enabled the date window filter will filter the schedule data table to items whose date is a specified number of days before and after the current date. This tool is targeted at those who prefer to view packages within a consistent date range window every time the page is loaded. See the **[Date Window Filter](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Date-Window-Filter)** article for more information on using this feature.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2022-8-3_10-50-8.png?version=1&modificationDate=1659541809164&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1100&height=187)
-   **BIM Area checkbox** - If BIM Areas are defined under Projects > Areas, checking the BIM Area checkbox will add a row for each BIM Area (Ex. Level 01 - Area A) and group packages under the BIM Areas.
    
-   **Expand All / Collapse All** - When the schedule is expanded, clicking the **Collapse All** button will collapse all package rows so that the package Phases (Office, Purchasing, Shop, Field) do not display.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-21-8.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540470634&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=458)
    
-   **Name Column Hierarchy** - The Name column hierarchy includes the following. See the screenshot at the top of this section:
    
    1.  **Project name** - (Ex. GTP - ITM - CAD - Master).
        
        1.  The Project row's Start Date and End Date are associated with the Project Target Start Date and Target End Dates Admin > Company > Projects.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-23_10-24-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1629732241658&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=750&height=325)
            
        2.  The project row includes 2 different Gantt bars:
            
            1.  **Thin multicolored bar** - The Project Target Start Date and Target End Date are represented by the colored thinner bar in the project row.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-23_10-24-59.png?version=1&modificationDate=1629732300965&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=886&height=250)
                
                1.  **Red** \- Indicates the time period before any package phase in the project has a Phase Start Date.
                2.  **Green** \- Indicates the time period when at least one package has a Phase Start Date.
                3.  **Yellow** \- Indicates the time period after any package phase in the project has a Phase Start Date.
                4.  **Start Date and End Date column dates** - The Start Date (6/15/2021) and End Date (9/28/2021) in the project row correspond to the thin bar (Project Target Start Date and Target End Date).
            2.  **Thick black bar** - All of the Project’s Package Phase Start Dates and Lead Days are represented by a thicker black bar in the project row.
    2.  **BIM Area** - If a BIM Area is checked and defined it will display (Ex. Level 01 - Area A)
        
    3.  **Package Number and Name** - (Ex. GTP001-PPF-001-L01 A)
        
    4.  **Phase** - Package Phases (Office, Purchasing, Shop, Field)
        
-   **Gantt chart bars** - Gantt chart bars are color-coded based on the package's Tracking Status.
-   **Today and Current Date Line** - The **Current Date Line** is indicated by a blue dashed line from the date to the bottom of the chart. Click the **Today** button to jump to the Current Date Line.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-21-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540514274&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=272)
    
-   **Center Gantt chart on a selected row** - To focus the Gantt chart on a row, click the row. The row will highlight green and the Phase bar will be centered in the Gantt chart.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-22-36.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540557431&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=750&height=333)
-   **Weekend dates** - The Weekend date columns are highlighted in light blue. These are ignored for business day calculations. Moving or resizing a Gantt bar will automatically adjust for the weekend.
    
-   **Holiday dates** - The Holiday date columns are highlighted in light red. A Holiday is treated as a business day.
    
-   **Sort** \- Packages can be sorted in Ascending or Descending order by Name, Start Date, End Date, or Duration. For example, to sort packages by End Date:
    
    1.  Click the column header. The packages will sort. Click again to sort in the opposite direction.
        
    2.  Click the 3-dots within the column header and select either Sort Ascending or Sort Descending.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-23-45.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540626214&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=139&height=250)
        
-   **Filter** - Packages can be filtered by Name, Start Date, End Date, or Duration. For example, to filter packages by Start Date:
    
    1.  Click the 3-dots within the column header and expand Filter.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-24-14.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540655880&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=350&height=361)
        
    2.  Expand the equality/inequality list and select an option.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-24-56.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540697362&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=224&height=250)  
          
        
    3.  Then enter or select the date and click **FILTER**.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-25-33.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628540735015&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=398&height=250)
        
    4.  The filter does not return if the page is refreshed.
        
    5.  A filter list can be further filtered by other columns.
        
-   When a package is created:
    
    1.  The package’s Start Date, End Date, and Duration for each phase will display as a row on the Schedule.
        
    2.  The minimum duration for any phase (Office, Purchasing, Shop, or Field) is 1 day.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/9044061/image2023-1-31_9-51-13.png?version=1&modificationDate=1675180275342&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        
    3.  Hover over any package to display progress statistics.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/9044061/image2023-1-31_9-53-17.png?version=1&modificationDate=1675180399013&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    4.  Hover over any phase to display Estimated and Earned hours as well as Planned and Actual Start/Finish dates.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/9044061/image2023-1-31_9-54-50.png?version=1&modificationDate=1675180491732&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
-   There are multiple ways to Edit Start Dates or End Dates in the Schedule:
    
    1.  **Package > Properties > Planning (Recommended)** - The most Lead Day information is available in the Package’s Planning area and is the best place to edit dates.
        
    2.  **Click and drag the entire Gantt bar** - To change the Start Date and End Date simultaneously, move the cursor over the bar and then click and drag the bar to the new date.
        
        1.  **Note**: If the Phase to the right (Ex. Shop) is locked (see the lock icon), then the Phase to the left (Purchasing) cannot be moved.  
            ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-9_15-31-22.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628541084332&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=301)
            
    3.  **Click and drag the left edge (Start Date) or right edge (End Date)** - Hover over the left or right edge until the cursor changes to horizontal arrows.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-11_8-26-3.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628688364543&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=372&height=39)  
        
    4.  **Edit** **Start Date or End Date Column Field** - Double-click the phase Start Date or End Date, edit the date by entering the date or using the calendar, click a different row to save. The Gantt chart will update.   
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2021-8-11_8-37-58.png?version=1&modificationDate=1628689080223&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=380&height=250) 
    5.  Once a date has been changed from the Schedule, refresh the Package’s > Properties > Planning page to display the updated information.   
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/9044061/image2022-5-19_15-35-34.png?version=1&modificationDate=1652992535897&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=860&height=250)

# Packages Status Board - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Status Board displays each package as a card on a Kanban board.

---
The Status Board displays each package as a card on a Kanban board.

-   1[Packages Status Board](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8781921/Packages+Status+Board#PackagesStatusBoard-PackagesStatusBoard)
    -   1.1[Color Code Cards](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8781921/Packages+Status+Board#PackagesStatusBoard-ColorCodeCards)
-   2[Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8781921/Packages+Status+Board#PackagesStatusBoard-Videos)

## Packages Status Board

The column headers are taken from your company's Tracking Statuses. Tracking Status updates can be made on this board by moving a card from one column to another. The tracking status for all assemblies and parts included in the moved package will update.  Each card contains information or links to information including:

-   **Package Name, View Details (Link)**
-   **Project Name**
-   **Due Date** - Targeted Due and calculated number of days until due
-   **Hours** - Estimate and Actual
-   **Tasks and Percent Complete** - Number of Tasks, Number of Tasks Done, the percent of tasks complete, number of Assemblies, and number of Parts.

1.  After a Division has been added to a package, the package will display on the **Packages > Status Board**. Here you can move individual package cards on a Kanban board (Issued for Fabrication, Issued for Purchasing, Purchased, etc.) to update the Division's queue. Each card includes Package details and links to package information.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/8781921/image2018-7-30_15-54-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1532984074243&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=848&height=386)
    
2.  **Filters**
    
    1.  **Project Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Projects.
        
    2.  **Model Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Models.
        
    3.  **Division Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Divisions.
    4.  **Status Filter** - Filter the list of packages by one or more Statuses.
    5.  **Category Filter** \- Filter list of packages by one or more Categories.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/8781921/image2023-1-26_9-13-38.png?version=1&modificationDate=1674746018778&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        
    6.  **Date Window Filter** - When enabled the date window filter will filter the schedule data table to items whose date is a specified number of days before and after the current date. This tool is targeted at those who prefer to view packages within a consistent date range window every time the page is loaded. See the **[Date Window Filter](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8749118/Packages+Dashboard#Date-Window-Filter)** article for more information on using this feature.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/8781921/image2022-8-3_10-49-21.png?version=1&modificationDate=1659541762397&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)

## Color Code Cards

**To color code status cards by project:**

1.  Go to **Admin** > **Company** > **Projects** and set the color for the project.
    
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/8781921/image2018-7-30_15-56-55.png?version=1&modificationDate=1532984217637&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=624&height=297)

See the Packages Module Overview webinar [**CSG Webinar: STRATUS In-Depth Series, The Packages Module**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/3309693/Packages#Packages-01/28/2021CSGWebinar:STRATUSIn-DepthSeries,ThePackagesModule(1:01:57)) for more information.

# Packages Viewer - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Packages > Viewer tab displays a package. A package displays when a users clicks a link from another page like a dashboard or by using the package filter tools (Ex. Project, Model, Package). The tab includes a 3D viewer section and the STRATUS Toolbar, and a detailed content section (Items, BOM, Cut Lists, STRATUS Sheet, Properties, etc.). In addition, the tab includes the ability to update Status, Division, Comment, and Hours.

---
The Packages > Viewer tab displays a package. A package displays when a users clicks a link from another page like a dashboard or by using the package filter tools (Ex. Project, Model, Package). The tab includes a 3D viewer section and the STRATUS Toolbar, and a detailed content section (Items, BOM, Cut Lists, STRATUS Sheet, Properties, etc.). In addition, the tab includes the ability to update Status, Division, Comment, and Hours.

-   1 [Open Package in the Packages > Viewer](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153/Packages+Viewer#Open-Package-in-the-Packages-%3E-Viewer)
