    -   7.7 [Add Attachment](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153/Packages+Viewer#Add-Attachment)
-   8 [Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153/Packages+Viewer#Videos)
    -   8.1 [01/28/2021 CSG Webinar: STRATUS In-Depth Series, The Packages Module](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153/Packages+Viewer#01%2F28%2F2021-CSG-Webinar%3A-STRATUS-In-Depth-Series%2C-The-Packages-Module)

## Open Package in the Packages > Viewer

There are several ways to open a package in the Packages > Viewer.

**Note**: STRATUS will recognize when users are working with a package and store the last opened or refreshed package as the active package. As a result, when the user clicks a link to an assembly, the active package will carryover and be selected in the Package drop-down. Otherwise, the Package will be set to Unspecified.

## Open Package from the Models Viewer

1.  In the Models > Viewer the Project and Model are selected.
    
2.  Under Filters > Packages, click the link to the package.
    
3.  The package will display with the same Project, Model, and Package selected. In Package's Details, if **Items** is selected as the default tab, then any of the package's Assemblies and Parts will display.  
    **Note**: In the Assemblies section, an assembly link can be clicked to open the assembly in the Assemblies > Viewer with the same Project, Model, and Package selected.
    

## Open Package from the Packages > Dashboard

1.  In the Packages > Dashboard, the Project and Model or ALL MODELS is selected.  **Note**: In this example, there are not additional filters for Division, Status, or Category.
    
2.  Click either the **Package Number** or **Package Name** link. **Note**: In this example, the Default Report is displaying.
    
3.  The package will display with the same Project, Model, and Package selected. In Package's Details, if **Items** is selected as the default tab, then any of the package's Assemblies and Parts will display.  
    **Note**: In the Assemblies section, an assembly link can be clicked to open the assembly in the Assemblies > Viewer with the same Project, Model, and Package selected.
    

## Open Package from the Assemblies > Dashboard

1.  In the Assemblies > Dashboard, the Project and Model or ALL MODELS is selected. **Note**: In this example, there are not additional filters for Package, Division, or Status.
    
2.  Click the Packages link. **Note**: In this example, the Default Assembly Report is displaying.
    
3.  The package will display with the same Project, Model, and Package selected. In Package's Details, if **Items** is selected as the default tab, then any of the package's Assemblies and Parts will display.  
    **Note**: In the Assemblies section, an assembly link can be clicked to open the assembly in the Assemblies > Viewer with the same Project, Model, and Package selected.
    

## Open Package from Package Drop-down

1.  In the Packages > Viewer with a Package already open, the Package control can be used to open a different package within the same Project and Model. Do one of the following:
    
    1.  Click the Package **drop-down** and select a different package.
        
    2.  Use the **Open Next** or **Open Previous** arrow buttons to open the next or previous package in alphabetic sort order.
        
2.  The selected package will display.
    

## Open Package by Scanning to the Package QR Code Scanned Page

See the [**Package QR Code Scanned**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#PackageQRCodeScanned "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1890025473/QR+Code+Scanned+Page#PackageQRCodeScanned") article for more information.

## Open Package from the Containers > Dashboard

Once a package has been added to a container, it will display under Containers > Dashboard.

1.  From the Containers > Dashboard, expand a Container to which a package has been added.
    
2.  Click the package name to open the package in a separate browser. 
    
3.  The package will display with the Project, Model, and Package selected. In Package's Details, if **Items** is selected as the default tab, then any of the package's Assemblies and Parts will display.  
    **Note**: In the Assemblies section, an assembly link can be clicked to open the assembly in the Assemblies > Viewer with the same Project, Model, and Package selected.
    

## Viewer Filtering

Once a package is opened, other packages can be located using the filtering options including drop-downs for Project, Model, View, and Package.

## Project

To locate a package in a different Project:

1.  Click the **Project** drop-down and either select the project or search for the project and the Packages > Dashboard will display.
    

## Model

To locate a package in a different Model within the Project:

1.  Click the Model drop-down and either select the model or search for the model. 
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/6467ccf6-0c9a-475f-8a7c-25dad5381ff9)
    
2.  When switching to a new model, STRATUS will not know which package you intend to open. Therefore, the first package (alphabetic) will be selected. If the model does not have a package, the Packages > Dashboard will display.
    

## View

By default, all published models include a 3D view. The person who publishes the model can select additional views including 2D views. 90% of the time the default view in the Packages Viewer will display the needed information. In some cases, like risers, the default view may not include all of the model parts and will need to be overridden.

**To change the view to a 2D View:**

1.  The model must be published with a 2D view.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/b7229f3a-6f82-4c08-8f12-0c50000801af)
    
2.  Select the 2D View and Click Ok when prompted. The 2D View will display. The following options available in a 3D View will be removed: STRATUS Toolbar, Search, Cube, Autodesk Toolbar features (Orbit, Model Browser, etc.).  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/0868d524-9fbb-46ed-8123-223b44f733fd)
    

### Package Viewer - View PDF Attachment

The Package's Viewer provides the ability to view a PDF attachment. This feature is useful for non-modeled packages. To use this feature:

1.  Under the Package’s > Attachments tab, attach one or more PDFs.
    
2.  Under the Package’s > Viewer tab, the PDF(s) will display. Use the View drop-down to view different PDF’s.
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/74f82920-75ff-4970-af97-908233a8611e)
    

## Package

See the [**Open Package from Package Drop-down**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153#PackagesViewer-OpenPackagefromPackageDrop-down "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/199983153#PackagesViewer-OpenPackagefromPackageDrop-down") section.

## 3D Viewer - Expand / Collapse

By default, the Packages > Viewer tab displays the 3D Viewer (left) and the package’s detailed content tabs (right). Clicking the expand to full screen button in either section will change both sections to full screen, one stacked on top of each other. 

Below are the mechanics of the Package Viewer expand / collapse feature:

1.  **Default View** - 3D Viewer (left) and package’s detailed content tabs (right) and expander/collapse buttons in both panels. Click a part or assembly in the viewer and it will be selected in the in the package’s detailed contents Items tab, or check an Assembly or Part in the Items tab and will be selected in the 3D Viewer.
    
2.  **Click the 3D panel expander** - The 3D View expands to full screen and the package’s detailed contents displays full screen below the 3D View. Click a part or assembly in the viewer and it will be selected in the in the package’s detailed contents Items tab, or check an Assembly or Part in the Items tab and will be selected in the 3D Viewer.
    
3.  **Click the collapse button in either the 3D Viewer or package’s detailed content tabs** - The default view will display. In this example, when the 3D View was expanded to full screen the user zoomed in on the assembly, added item numbers, and then collapsing the panels retained both.
    
4.  **Click the package’s detailed content tabs expander** - The package’s detailed contents display on top and the 3D view on the bottom. In this example, the BOM tab was clicked and the zoom and item numbers are retained from the previous example.
    

## 3D Viewer - Settings

Click the **Click to Change Settings** gear icon to access viewer **Settings**. See the [**Viewer Settings and Search**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001") article for more information.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/7be07d66-cfd4-4ace-ad32-8bb34b7ad319)

Settings in the Packages > Viewer include the following:

-   **Hidden Parts Shaded**
    
-   **Assembly Selection**
    
-   **Multiple Part Selection**
    
-   **Dynamic Tags**
    
-   **Decimal Inches / Feet Inches Toggle**
    

## 3D Viewer - Search for Parts and Assemblies

Click the Search icon to access the viewer's **Search**. See the [**Viewer Settings and Search**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2011136001") article for more information.

1.  Click the Search button.
    
2.  Click into the Search box. The gear icon will display. 
    
3.  Click the gear icon to display and configure the search settings.

See the See the Models > Viewer [**Display Modes**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#DisplayModes "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#DisplayModes") article for more information.

1.  Click the **Filters** option to further filter the package. **Note**: Each user’s last set of filters per model are stored. Filters for the Models Viewer are separate from the Packages Viewer filters. When the Packages Viewer is opened, a user can either manually (default) or automatically load their last session filter settings which is documented in the Models Viewer article. See the following for more information:
    
    1.  [**Filter Loading from Account Settings > Viewer Preferences**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#FilterLoadingfromAccountSettings%3EViewerPreferences "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#FilterLoadingfromAccountSettings%3EViewerPreferences")
        
    2.  [**Manually Load Last Session Filter Settings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969")
        
    3.  ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/690ceabd-dd1d-4b46-8758-c00e6ae9c398)
        

## Actions

See the Models > Viewer [**Actions**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#Actions "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#Actions") article for more information.

## Grid Offset Measurement

See the Models > Viewer [**Grid Offset Measurement**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#GridOffsetMeasurement "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#GridOffsetMeasurement") article for more information.

Click the **Grid Offset Measurement** tool for a digital tape measure and then select an item in the viewer. The tool will display the item’s dimension offset from grid line intersections. You can pick which level the tool is referencing and select which grid to measure in the drop-down. The distance to the X, Y grid line will display for point A and point B.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/0e529acd-60d1-4254-a726-5d78e0869aa6)

## Display Grid

See the Models > Viewer [**Display Grid**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#DisplayGrid "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969/Models+Viewer#DisplayGrid") article for more information.

Click the **Display Grid** tool to display the model grid. The RVT or DWG would need to have been published with a grid.  

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/1cd5d56d-9f3a-41d2-a3b5-fadc8ce48ae6)

## Package Tracking

The following tracking data can be entered and applied at anytime and any number of fields (Ex. Status, Hours, and Cost Type) can be updated.

## Status

Changing the Status of a package will also change the status of all parts and assemblies included in the package.

To change the Status of a package in the Packages > Viewer:

1.  Do one of the following:
    
    1.  Click the Status **drop-down**.
        
        1.  Enter text to search for status and/or select a status.
            
    2.  Click the **Next Tracking Status** button. The next status in sequence order will be selected.
        
2.  Once selected, click the **Apply** button to save. The status of the package and all parts and assemblies included in the package will be updated.
    

**A package's Status can be changed on the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer 
    
2.  Scan
    

## Division

A **Division** is a name for a department, person, or group that processes work packages and is specific to your company’s workflow, and is used to filter data tables. The future vision for Divisions is to use divisions as discreet business units that most closely align to a single cost code or group of cost codes. A Division is required when defining a Station. See the [**Project Divisions (Admin)**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2038333441 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2038333441") article for information about Project-level Divisions.

To change the Division of a package in the Packages > Viewer:

1.  Click the Division drop-down and either select the division or search for the division.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/e4558b02-f316-438a-b744-88c3bb1e236b)
    
2.  Once selected, click the **Apply** button to save.
    

**Division Not Assigned to the Package**

If a Division has not been assigned to a package the Division will not display. For example:

1.  When this package was changed to the Issued tracking status, a Division was not assigned. As a result, the Division display is blank inside the brackets.
    
2.  To update the Division, click the Tracking tab, select the Status and then select the Division.
    
3.  The Division will display.
    
4.  **Notes**:
    
    1.  If a Division is not selectable, it means that a Division has not been checked under the Tracking Status Group on the Admin > Company > Tracking Statuses page. Check a checkbox and then refresh the Tracking tab to make a Division selectable.
        
    2.  Check that a Division has been defined for the checkbox selected (above) under Admin > Company > Divisions.
        

**A Division can be added to a package from the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer
    
2.  Scan
    

Comments can be added to a package in the following ways:

1.  Manually added to a package on the Packages > Viewer or Scan page.
    
2.  Automatically when the package is added to a Container. Comments display on the package's Tracking tab.  The source container name (Ex. Truck) will be included in the tracking log entry comment.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/bd236093-2030-4443-a1a8-e802a228b1ae)
    

**Comments can be added to a package from the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer
    
2.  Scan
    
3.  Container - When a package is added to a container, a comment is automatically recorded.
    

## Hours

Hours entered and applied to a package will used for Actual Hours reporting. By default, Actual Hours display on the Packages > Dashboard > Default report. Hours can also be extracted into reports using the following:

-   STRATUS.Package.HoursActual
    
-   STRATUS.Package.TrackingHours
    
-   STRATUS.Package.TrackingStatusHoursLog
    

To add hours to a package in the Packages > Viewer:

1.  Open the package.
    
2.  Enter a numeric value in the Hours field.
    
3.  Once entered, click the **Apply** button to save.
    

**Hours can be added to a package from the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer
    
2.  Scan
    
3.  Container - When a package is added to a container, Hours can be entered in the Tracking section.
    

## Cost Type

Cost Type can be added to a package:

1.  Click the Cost Type drop-down and either select the Cost Type or search for the Cost Type.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/d55d2bde-bb03-4e46-bbbe-3b25f295bfe9)
    
2.  Once selected, click the **Apply** button to save.
    

**Cost Type can be added to a package from the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer
    
2.  Scan
    
3.  Container - When a package is added to a container, Cost Type can be entered in the Tracking section.
    

## Capture Image 

An image using the devices camera can be added to the package.

To Capture an Image:

1.  Click the Capture Image button. The device must have a camera.
    
2.  All the camera to be used.
    
3.  Click Capture Image. 
    
4.  Once the image is captured, click the **Apply** button. The Confirm File Name dialog will display. 
    
5.  Accept or edit the File Name and click **Ok**.
    
6.  The image is saved an will be accessible in the Attachments and Tracking tabs.
    

## Add Attachment

An Attachment can be added to a package in several locations. The process is the same for all.

See the [**Attachments**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/2081619969") article for more information.

**An Attachment can be added to a package from the following pages:**

1.  Packages > Viewer > Add Attachment in the Tracking row.
    
2.  Packages > Viewer > Items > Assemblies or Parts > Attachments
    
3.  Packages > Viewer > Attachments
    
4.  Packages > Viewer > Tracking (tab)
    
5.  Packages > Dashboard

# Profile - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Profile tab provides users with options to manage their Date & Time, Viewer Preferences, Package Dashboard Preferences, and their badge Avatar.

---
The Profile tab provides users with options to manage their Date & Time, Viewer Preferences, Package Dashboard Preferences, and their badge Avatar.

-   1 [Date & Time](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile#Date-%26-Time)
-   2 [Viewer Preferences](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile#Viewer-Preferences)
    -   2.1 [Configure Account Viewer Preferences](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile#Configure-Account-Viewer-Preferences)
-   3 [Package Dashboard Preferences](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile#Package-Dashboard-Preferences)
-   4 [Badge Avatar](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile#Badge-Avatar)

## Date & Time

The Date & Time section controls how dates and times are displayed per user.

To use this feature:

1.  Open the Profile page by clicking your badge > Account Settings > Profile.
    
2.  By default, Date & Time settings are configured as follows:
    
3.  To change settings:
    
    1.  **Time Zone** - Select your time zone.
        
    2.  **Long Date** - The selected format populates the STRATUS.Report.CurrentDateLong field. Examples:
        
        1.  **dddd, MMMM d, yyyy** = Monday, October 9, 2023
            
        2.  **MMMM d, yyyy** = October 9, 2023
            
        3.  **dddd, d MMMM, yyyy** = Monday, 9 October, 2023
            
        4.  **d MMMM, yyyy** = 9 October, 2023
            
    3.  **Date** \- Select your preferred date display.
        
    4.  **Time** \- Select your preferred time display.
        
    5.  **System** \= Select either 24 hour or 12 hour (includes AM and PM after the time.)
        
4.  **Note:** A sample of any displays at the bottom of the Date & Time section.
    
5.  Click **Save** to save any changes.
    
6.  Refresh any open page to display the configured Date & Time settings.
    
    1.  Submit a [**STRATUS Service Desk**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3 "https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/3") desk ticket if you find a scenario that does not display the date/time as configured.
        

## Viewer Preferences

Each user can set their Account Viewer Preferences to either manually apply or automatically apply the last session’s settings (STRATUS Filters and Forge settings). By default, all options are unchecked. For more information on how these settings impact the viewers (Models, Packages, Assemblies), see the [**Filter Loading from Account Settings > Viewer Preferences**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-FilterLoadingfromAccountSettings%3EViewerPreferences "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-FilterLoadingfromAccountSettings%3EViewerPreferences") article for more information.

### Configure Account Viewer Preferences

Each user can set their account **Viewer Preferences** to either manually apply or automatically apply the last session’s settings. By default, all options are unchecked (manually apply in the viewer). To change settings:

1.  Click the Badge (upper right corner) > Account Settings > Profile > **Viewer Preferences**.
    
2.  The **Save Autodesk viewer settings (all viewers)** checkbox:
    
    1.  **Checked** - When checked, the last Autodesk Forge session settings will be loaded. This setting applies globally to all viewers (Models, Packages, Assemblies) and all models.
        
    2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked, Autodesk Forge settings will reset after each session.
        
3.  The **Apply last session filter settings** checkboxes:
    
    1.  **Models Viewer** - Each model has individual filter settings per user.
        
        1.  **Checked** - When checked the user’s last Model Viewer > Filter settings will be automatically loaded when the model opens in the Models Viewer. See the [**Automatically Load Last Session Filter Settings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-AutomaticallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-AutomaticallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings") section for more information. In addition, it will take more time for models to load.
            
        2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked, the user’s filter settings will still be stored, however, the filter settings will not be automatically loaded. See the [**Manually Load Last Session Filter Settings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-ManuallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-ManuallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings") section for more information. In addition, it will take less time for models to load than if the option is checked.
            
    2.  **Packages Viewer** - Each model has individual filter settings per user. The Package filter settings apply to all the model’s packages.
        
        1.  **Checked** - When checked the last Packages > Filter settings will be automatically loaded when a package is opened in the Packages Viewer. See the [**Automatically Load Last Session Filter Settings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-AutomaticallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-AutomaticallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings") section for more information.
            
        2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked, the user’s filter settings will still be stored, however, the filter settings will not be automatically loaded. See the [**Manually Load Last Session Filter Settings**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-ManuallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings "/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/9043969#ModelsViewer-ManuallyLoadLastSessionFilterSettings") section for more information.
            
    3.  **Assemblies Viewer (References filter only)** - The Assemblies Viewer checkbox only applies to the References filter. See the **References and Clip Settings** section of the [**Filters**](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/1953858294/Profile# "#") article for more information.
        
        1.  **Checked** - When checked the last Filters > References setting will be stored.
            
        2.  **Unchecked** - When unchecked, Filters > References will not be stored.
            
    4.  Click **Save** if any changes are made.
        

## Package Dashboard Preferences

When checked, the **Allow Package Dashboard Filter Restore** option tells STRATUS to restore the user’s filter options on the Packages > Dashboard after a page refresh or in their next session. We call it sticky filters.

## Badge Avatar

To change your badge Avatar:

1.  Click the **Browse** button, locate the image file, and click Upload.
    
2.  Once uploaded the image will display as your badge.

# Scan - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Scan page is used for "continuous" QR scanning and tracking status updates. With each scan, the select Status, Division, Comment, Hours, and Cost Type will be applied to the scanned QR code for the part, assembly, or package.  The Scan page for updating tracking statuses works with hand held scanner input devices connected to a computer logged into STRATUS as well as iPad and table cameras.

---
The Scan page is used for "continuous" QR scanning and tracking status updates. With each scan, the select Status, Division, Comment, Hours, and Cost Type will be applied to the scanned QR code for the part, assembly, or package.  The Scan page for updating tracking statuses works with hand held scanner input devices connected to a computer logged into STRATUS as well as iPad and table cameras. 

-   1[Videos](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-Videos)
    -   1.1[STRATUS 09-26-19 Implementation Webinar - QR Code Workflows (30:08)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-STRATUS09-26-19ImplementationWebinar-QRCodeWorkflows(30%3A08))
    -   1.2[Video: Phone Status Updates (0:45)](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-Video%3APhoneStatusUpdates(0%3A45))
-   2[Configuration and Use](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-ConfigurationandUse)
    -   2.1[To use the Scan page](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-TousetheScanpage)
    -   2.2[To access information about the scanned item](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-Toaccessinformationaboutthescanneditem)
    -   2.3[QR Code Scanning in STRATUS](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/158040194/Scan#Scan-QRCodeScanninginSTRATUS)

## Videos

## STRATUS 09-26-19 Implementation Webinar - QR Code Workflows (30:08)  

****************************************************************************************************************************<iframe allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true" data-hasbody="false" data-macro-id="c7a851bf-face-4e5d-8232-3835f855dcfd" data-macro-name="widget" frameborder="0" height="364" mozallowfullscreen="" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/362660942?h=embed" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="640"></iframe>****************************************************************************************************************************

## Video: Phone Status Updates (0:45)

****************************************************************************************************************************<iframe allowfullscreen="" allowtransparency="true" data-hasbody="false" data-macro-id="c9448be5-46af-4521-a67e-695654540f6a" data-macro-name="widget" frameborder="0" height="364" mozallowfullscreen="" src="https://player.vimeo.com/video/365129753?h=embed" webkitallowfullscreen="" width="640"></iframe>****************************************************************************************************************************

## Configuration and Use

## To use the Scan page

1.  Do one of the following to connect between STRATUS and the Scanner:
    1.  Connect a wired or Bluetooth hand Handheld scanner to a device where you have logged into STRATUS and have opened the Scan page.
    2.  Connect with a Bluetooth scanner tethered to phone or tablet as input device where you have logged into STRATUS and have opened the Scan page.
    3.  Connect with an iPad or Tablet computer that has a built-in camera where you have logged into STRATUS and have opened the Scan page.
2.  On the Scan page, set the following. All settings are optional as any data can be updated.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2023-10-19_10-35-37.png?version=1&modificationDate=1697729738207&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    1.  **Add Assembly on Scan (Optional)** - By checking this checkbox, when the part is contained in an assembly, any changes made to the Status will be applied to all parts in the assembly.  
        For example: 
        1.  The Tracking Status of all parts in this assembly are set to Ordered.![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2023-10-19_10-44-0.png?version=1&modificationDate=1697730241907&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        2.  After opening the Scan page, updating the desired settings, and clicking either **Begin Scan** button, the page will look similar to the following:![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2023-10-19_10-45-39.png?version=1&modificationDate=1697730340302&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
        3.  With the page active (click in any white space if you have changed tabs), scan the QR Code of any part in the assembly.
            1.  The Scan page will update similar to the following:![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2023-10-19_10-48-21.png?version=1&modificationDate=1697730502535&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
            2.  The assemblies Tracking Status will be updated:![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2023-10-19_10-49-39.png?version=1&modificationDate=1697730580455&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
    2.  **Status (Optional)** - Select the Status to be set after the scan is made. The list of Divisions will be filtered.
    3.  **Division (Optional)** - Select the Division to be set after the scan is made.
    4.  **Comment**  **(Optional)** - Enter a comment to display on the Tracking row after the scan is made.
    5.  **Hours**  **(Optional)** - Enter hours to be calculated after the scan is made.
    6.  ****Cost Type**** **(Optional)** - Select the Cost Type to be set after the scan is made.
3.  Select a Begin Scan option:
    1.  If using option 1a, above, click the **Begin Scan (Handheld)** button.
    2.  If using option 1b or 1c above, click the **Begin Scan (Camera)** button.
4.  **Scan the QR code**.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/attachments/158040194/image2018-6-19_9-7-32.png?version=1&modificationDate=1529417254705&cacheVersion=1&api=v2)
5.  The tracking table will populate. If you have selected a tracking status that is not applicable to the type of code scanned, an annoying error sound will clank and an “Unrecognized Code” error message will display. Otherwise, the tracking status will update in the grid.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2020-6-23_11-55-36.png?version=1&modificationDate=1592931337486&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1300&height=250)
6.  Click the **Change Status** button to apply a different tracking status to the parts, assemblies, or packages to be scanned next.
7.  Click the **Clear** button to clear all scanned rows on the Scan page. Click the Remove Item button to remove an individual item.

## To access information about the scanned item

1.  Once a QR code has been scanned, a row of information will display about the scanned part including the QR code.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2020-6-23_11-55-36.png?version=1&modificationDate=1592931337486&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1300&height=250)
2.  Click the QR code or scan the QR code with a tablet or smart phone that is logged into STRATUS.  An item landing page similar to the following will display.  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2020-6-23_12-55-6.png?version=1&modificationDate=1592934907555&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=432)
3.  Here you have access to:
    1.  The **Tracking** status history.
    2.  The **View Assembly** where the Assemblies Viewer will display, or,  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2018-8-8_16-43-4.png?version=1&modificationDate=1533764586572&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=565&height=337)
    3.  The **View Container** button where the Containers page displays, or,   
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2020-6-23_12-57-27.png?version=1&modificationDate=1592935048601&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=619&height=270)
    4.  The **View Location** button where the item is Isolated in the **Models Viewer** with the “Show hidden parts shaded” checkbox checked.  
        ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2018-8-8_16-43-42.png?version=1&modificationDate=1533764623526&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=567&height=340)

## QR Code Scanning in STRATUS

The graphic below shows the types of QR codes that can be generated and where they are scanned in STRATUS. See the STRATUS 09-26-19 Implementation Webinar (QR Code Workflows 30:08) for more information.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/158040194/image2019-9-27_8-24-21.png?version=1&modificationDate=1569590696878&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1006&height=620)

# Services (Admin) - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> For each project, Services from all published models (Revit and AutoCAD) can be loaded and optionally a cost code can be manually entered for each.

---
For each project, Services from all published models (Revit and AutoCAD) can be loaded and optionally a cost code can be manually entered for each.

Load services under Admin > Project > Services. Click the **Refresh** button to refresh the list. Any manually entered cost codes will be retained after a Refresh. If the BOM Service Name is not displaying as expected in STRATUS, click the Refresh  button to refresh the list.

-   1[Refresh Services](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/317030401/Services+Admin#Services(Admin)-RefreshServices)

## Refresh Services

To Refresh Services:

1.  Under **Projects** > **Services**, click the **Refresh Services** button. A new row will display. STRATUS will extract and list all services from published models (Revit and AutoCAD).  
    ![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/317030401/image2020-1-14_8-59-52.png?version=1&modificationDate=1579013994332&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=681&height=447)

# Shipping Addresses (Admin) - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Shipping Addresses information is configured per project and can be created or imported.

---
Shipping Addresses information is configured per project and can be created or imported.

-   1 [New Shipping Address](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/742916377/Shipping+Addresses+Admin#New-Shipping-Address)
-   2 [Reports](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/742916377/Shipping+Addresses+Admin#Reports)
-   3 [Report Fields](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/742916377/Shipping+Addresses+Admin#Report-Fields)
-   4 [Template](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/742916377/Shipping+Addresses+Admin#Template)
-   5 [Select Project Shipping Address on Report](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/742916377/Shipping+Addresses+Admin#Select-Project-Shipping-Address-on-Report)

## New Shipping Address

To create a New Shipping Address:

1.  Under **Projects** > **Shipping Addresses**, click the **New Shipping Address** button. A new row will display. 
    
    1.  **Default (Optional)**\- Select one default shipping address. When checked, the checked Shipping Address will be automatically selected for all models on the Models > Dashboard, Shipping Address column.
        
    2.  **Address Name (Required)** - Enter the name of the Shipping Address. This will display on all Purchasing activities.
        
    3.  **Attention** **(Optional)** \- If "Attention" should be used in the address, enter that information here.
        
    4.  **Address 1 (Required)**\- Enter the shipping address line 1.
        
    5.  **Address 2 (Optional)** - Enter the shipping address line 2.
        
    6.  **City (Required)**\- Enter the shipping address city.
        
    7.  **State (Required)**\- Enter the shipping address state.
        
    8.  **Zip (Required)**\- Enter the shipping address zip code.
        
    9.  **Phone** **(Optional)** \- Enter the phone number for the contact or office that can be called by the supplier to clarify questions.
        
    10.  **Instructions (Optional)** - Enter any instructions that all shipments should include.
        
2.  Click **Save** when Done. Below is an example. 
    

## Reports

Reports can be setup for the following Item Types:

![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/898b9e05-6ff7-42ac-a2c2-6b456a780f2f)

1.  Assembly
    
2.  Container
    
3.  Container Details
    
4.  Package
    
5.  Package Details
    
6.  Part
    

## Report Fields

In each report, the following Report Fields are available:

-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Name
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Address1
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Address2
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.City
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.State
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Zip
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Attention
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Instructions
    
-   STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress.Phone
    

## Template

Users can reference the STRATUS.Model.ShippingAddress Report Fields on the following Template Types:

-   Package Sheet
    
-   Assemblies Sheet
    
-   Package BOM
    
-   Container Details
    

## Select Project Shipping Address on Report

When more than one shipping address exists for a project, a user can select which shipping address to use when running a BOM report.

1.  **To add Shipping Address information to a project**, under Projects, select the project, click the Shipping Addresses tab, and then add one or more Shipping Addresses.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/4cb6b08a-4e75-46eb-b61f-f3cff10fdb18)
    
2.  **To add the Shipping Address Report Fields to a template**, under Admin > Company > Templates, create or select a BOM template where the Template Type is Bill of Materials and then add Report Fields that include .ShippingAddress.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/fc651727-656b-4969-8ca3-354d2692fa26)
    
3.  To select a shipping address for a BOM report, go a Package’s BOM tab, select a report and click the download button. The **Select Report Options** dialog similar to the following will display. Select the Shipping Address.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/bae97ee1-f4b3-4d7c-ac79-a399a29b9995)
    
4.  The report will display the .ShippingAddress report fields as configured on the template.  
    
    ![](blob:https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/fc746444-c734-4987-8d57-68c59f6cac36)

# Shops Dashboard - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> The Shops Dashboard displays the number of Cut Lists and Tasks for each Station. For each Station under Admin > Company > Stations, a Division is assigned which is used to organize the display in the Shop drop-down list.

---
The Shops Dashboard displays the number of Cut Lists and Tasks for each Station. For each Station under Admin > Company > Stations, a **Division** is assigned which is used to organize the display in the Shop drop-down list. 

-   1[Shop Dashboard](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014/Shops+Dashboard#ShopsDashboard-ShopDashboard)
    -   1.1[Sign In to a Shop Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014/Shops+Dashboard#ShopsDashboard-SignIntoaShopStation)
-   2[Station Tool](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014/Shops+Dashboard#ShopsDashboard-StationTool)
-   3[Station Tasks](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/8913014/Shops+Dashboard#ShopsDashboard-StationTasks)

## Shop Dashboard

Initially, the Shops Dashboard displays the number of Cut Lists and Tasks for each Station. Under Admin > Company > Stations, each Station includes an assigned **Division** which displays in the Shop drop-down list (Ex. Pipe Shop). When a Shop has a task whose status is either "To Do" or "In Progress" it will display.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/8913014/image2021-12-9_10-36-9.png?version=1&modificationDate=1639067770239&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=437)

## Sign In to a Shop Station

See the **[Sign In to a Shop Station](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/SK/pages/215220408/Station+Admin#Station(Admin)-SignIntoaShopStation)** section of the Station (Admin) article for more information.

## Station Tool

Click the station name (Ex. TigerStop - TD) and then click the Tool tab to view current queues for the station's tool. The list can be sorted and filtered.

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/8913014/image2021-12-9_10-40-18.png?version=1&modificationDate=1639068020025&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=384) 

**Information includes:**

-   **Requested** - The date/time the cut list was sent to the queue.
-   **Project** - The cut list's project.
-   **Package** - The cut list's package.
-   **Material** - The material included in the cut list.
-   **Size** - The size or diameter of the cut list.
-   **Total Length** - The total length of all items in the cut list.
-   **\# Items** - The total number of items in the cut list.
-   **Status** - The status of the cut list. If cutting with a TigerStop, the status is updated in real-time.
-   **Print Labels** - Prints labels for the selected cut list.
-   **Unassign from Station** - To remove the cut list from this station, click the **Unassign from Station** button. The progress of the cut list is retained so parts already cut will not be cut a second time when resent to a cutting station. In addition, the cut list will be retained on the Cut Lists tab ready to be sent to a station. The **Unassign from Station** is also available on the Packages > Cut List page.

## Station Tasks

Click the station name (Ex. TigerStop - TD) and then click the Tasks tab to view current queues for the station's Tasks.

-   If tasks were generated under the Packages > Tasks tab, then they will display here.
-   Only tasks whose task status is "To Do" or "In Progress" will display.  
    

![](https://gtpservices.atlassian.net/wiki/download/thumbnails/8913014/image2021-12-9_10-43-5.png?version=1&modificationDate=1639068186857&cacheVersion=1&api=v2&width=1000&height=390)

# Stratus In The Browser - STRATUS Knowledge Base - Confluence

> ## Excerpt
> Atlassian uses cookies to improve your browsing experience, perform analytics and research, and conduct advertising. Accept all cookies to indicate that you agree to our use of cookies on your device. Atlassian cookies and tracking notice, (opens new window)

---
Atlassian uses cookies to improve your browsing experience, perform analytics and research, and conduct advertising. Accept all cookies to indicate that you agree to our use of cookies on your device. [Atlassian cookies and tracking notice, (opens new window)](https://www.atlassian.com/legal/cookies)
